import { baseRequest } from '@/utils/request'

const request = (url, ...arg) => baseRequest(`/api/services/app/FlowDefinition/` + url, ...arg)

/**
 * 流程管理API
 */
export default {
    /**
     * 获取流程定义分页列表
     * @param {Object} data 查询参数
     */
    getPageList(data) {
        return request('GetPageList', data, 'get')
    },

    /**
     * 获取所有流程定义列表（不分页）
     */
    getAllList() {
        return request('GetAllList', null, 'get')
    },

    /**
     * 获取流程定义详情
     * @param {Object} data { id: string }
     */
    getById(data) {
        return request('GetById', data, 'get')
    },

    /**
     * 获取流程配置JSON
     * @param {Object} data { flowDefId: string }
     */
    getFlowConfig(data) {
        return request('GetFlowConfig', data, 'get')
    },

    /**
     * 创建流程定义
     * @param {Object} data 流程数据
     */
    create(data) {
        return request('Create', data, 'post')
    },

    /**
     * 更新流程定义
     * @param {Object} data 流程数据
     */
    updateById(data) {
        return request('UpdateById', data, 'put')
    },

    /**
     * 保存或更新流程定义（兼容旧版）
     * @param {Object} data 流程数据
     */
    saveOrUpdate(data) {
        if (data.workFlowDef?.id) {
            data.id = data.workFlowDef?.id
            return request('UpdateById', data, 'put')
        } else {
            return request('Create', data, 'post')
        }
    },

    /**
     * 删除流程定义
     * @param {Object} data { id: string }
     */
    deleteByIds(data) {
        return request('DeleteByIds', data, 'delete')
    },


    /**
     * 启用流程
     * @param {Object} data { id: string }
     */
    enableFlow(data) {
        return request('EnableById', { id: data.id }, 'put')
    },

    /**
     * 停用流程
     * @param {Object} data { id: string }
     */
    freezeFlow(data) {
        return request('FreezeById', { id: data.id }, 'put')
    },

    /**
     * 更改流程状态（启用/停用）
     * @param {Object} data { id: string, status: number }
     */
    changeStatus(data) {
        return request('ChangeStatus', data, 'put')
    },

    /**
     * 更新工作台显示状态
     * @param {Object} data { id: string, showInWorkbench: boolean }
     */
    updateWorkbenchShow(data) {
        return request('UpdateWorkbenchShow', data, 'put')
    },


    /**
     * 获取流程版本历史
     * @param {Object} data { flowDefId: string }
     */
    getFlowHistory(data) {
        return request('GetFlowHistory', data, 'get')
    },

    /**
     * 回滚到指定版本
     * @param {Object} data { flowDefId: string, version: number }
     */
    rollbackToVersion(data) {
        return request('RollbackToVersion', data, 'post')
    },

    /**
     * 复制流程
     * @param {Object} data { id: string, name: string }
     */
    copyFlow(data) {
        return request('CopyFlow', data, 'post')
    },

    /**
     * 导出流程定义
     * @param {Object} data { id: string }
     */
    exportFlow(data) {
        return request('ExportFlow', data, 'get')
    },

    /**
     * 导入流程定义
     * @param {Object} data FormData
     */
    importFlow(data) {
        return request('ImportFlow', data, 'post')
    },

    /**
     * 验证流程定义
     * @param {Object} data 流程数据
     */
    validateFlow(data) {
        return request('ValidateFlow', data, 'post')
    },

    /**
     * 获取流程统计数据
     * @param {Object} data { id: string }
     */
    getFlowStatistics(data) {
        return request('GetFlowStatistics', data, 'get')
    },

    /**
     * 获取所有启用的流程（用于选择器）
     */
    getEnabledFlowsForSelector() {
        return request('GetEnabledFlowsForSelector', null, 'get')
    },

    /**
     * 检查流程名称是否已存在
     * @param {Object} data { name: string, excludeId: string }
     */
    checkNameExists(data) {
        return request('CheckNameExists', data, 'get')
    }
}



flow/common/ArrayUtil.js

/**
 * 删除某个元素
 *
 * @param {Array} arr
 * @param {String} key
 * @param {String} value
 */
function remove(arr, key, value) {
  let idx = -1;
  for (let i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
    if (arr[i][key] == value) {
      idx = i;
      break;
    }
  }

  if (idx != -1) {
    arr.splice(idx, 1);
  }
}

/**
 * 根据指定属性值获取某个元素
 *
 * @param {Array} arr
 * @param {String} key
 * @param {String} val
 */
function get(arr, key, val) {
  for (let i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
    if (arr[i][key] == val) return arr[i];
  }
  return {};
}

/**
 * 是否为数组
 *
 * @param {Object} obj
 * @returns
 */
function isArray(obj) {
  return Array.isArray(obj);
}

/**
 * 数组去重
 *
 * @param {*} arr
 * @param {*} field
 * @returns
 */
function distinct(arr, field) {
  var obj = {};
  arr = arr.reduce(function (item, next) {
    obj[next[field]] ? "" : (obj[next[field]] = true && item.push(next));
    return item;
  }, []);
  return arr;
}

/**
 * 两个数组的交集
 *
 * @param {*} a
 * @param {*} b
 * @returns
 */
function intersection(a, b) {
  return a.filter((v) => b.includes(v));
}

/**
 * 数组去重
 *
 * @param {Array} arr
 * @returns
 */
const unique = (arr) => {
  const res = new Map();
  return arr.filter((arr) => !res.has(arr) && res.set(arr, 1));
};

export default { remove, get, isArray, distinct, intersection, unique };

flow/common/FlowFormula.js

import { WIDGET } from "@/components/flow/common/FlowConstant";
import ObjectUtil from "@/components/flow/common/ObjectUtil";

/**
 * 校验表单组件的公式
 *
 * @param {Array} widgets
 * @returns 公式有错误的组件名称列表
 */
export const formulaWidgetVerify = (widgets) => {
  let formulaErrorWidgetNameList = [];
  if (!(widgets && widgets.length)) return formulaErrorWidgetNameList;

  widgets.forEach((widget) => {
    let { name, type, details, formulaItems } = widget;
    if (type == WIDGET.DETAIL) {
      // 筛选出可以作为公式的明细组件
      let formulaDetailWidgetKv = {};
      let formulaDetailWidgets = (details || []).filter((i) => {
        let { required, type, label, name } = i;
        if (required && [WIDGET.NUMBER, WIDGET.MONEY].includes(type)) {
          formulaDetailWidgetKv[name] = label;
        }
        return type == WIDGET.FORMULA;
      });

      // 校验明细组件的单项公式
      (formulaItems || []).forEach((i) => {
        let { value } = i;
        if (value.length <= 1) return; // 符号的长度为1，剔除掉，这里只校验组件的引用
        if (formulaDetailWidgetKv.hasOwnProperty(value)) {
          i.name = formulaDetailWidgetKv[value]; // 更新被引用组件的名称
        } else {
          formulaErrorWidgetNameList.push(name);
        }
      });

      (formulaDetailWidgets || []).forEach((formulaDetailWidget) => {
        let { formulaItems, name: formulaDetailName } = formulaDetailWidget;
        (formulaItems || []).forEach((i) => {
          let { value } = i;
          if (value.length <= 1) return; // 符号的长度为1，剔除掉，这里只校验组件的引用
          if (formulaDetailWidgetKv.hasOwnProperty(value)) {
            i.name = formulaDetailWidgetKv[value]; // 更新被引用组件的名称
          } else {
            formulaErrorWidgetNameList.push(formulaDetailName);
          }
        });
      });
    } else if (type == WIDGET.FORMULA && formulaItems && formulaItems.length) {
      // 筛选出可以作为公式的组件
      let formulaWidgetKv = {};
      widgets.forEach((widget) => {
        let { required, type, label, name } = widget;
        if ((required && [WIDGET.NUMBER, WIDGET.MONEY].includes(type)) || type == WIDGET.DETAIL) {
          formulaWidgetKv[name] = label;
        }
      });

      formulaItems.forEach((i) => {
        let { value } = i;
        if (value.length <= 1) return; // 符号的长度为1，剔除掉，这里只校验组件的引用
        if (formulaWidgetKv.hasOwnProperty(value)) {
          i.name = formulaWidgetKv[value]; // 更新被引用组件的名称
        } else {
          formulaErrorWidgetNameList.push(name);
        }
      });
    }
  });
  return formulaErrorWidgetNameList;
};

/**
 * 初始化公式组件公式
 *
 * @param {Array} widgets
 */
export const initWidgetFormula = (widgets) => {
  (widgets || []).forEach((widget) => {
    let { type, formulaItems, details } = widget;
    if ([WIDGET.DETAIL, WIDGET.FORMULA].includes(type) && !!formulaItems && formulaItems.length) {
      widget.formula = "${" + formulaItems.map((i) => i.value).join("") + "}";
      if (type == WIDGET.FORMULA) {
        widget.placeholder = formulaItems.map((i) => i.name).join("");
      }
    }

    if (type == WIDGET.DETAIL && !!details && details.length) {
      initWidgetFormula(details);
    }
  });
};

/**
 * 解析公式表达式中的组件名称
 *
 * @param {String} formula
 */
export const listFormulaWidgetNames = (formula) => {
  if (!ObjectUtil.isNotEmpty(formula)) return [];
  const regex = /[A-Z]+_\d{18}/g;
  const matches = formula.match(regex);
  return matches || [];
};

/**
 *计算公式结果
 *
 * @param {String} formula
 * @param {Object} vars
 * @returns
 */
export const formulaEval = (formula, vars) => {
  if (!ObjectUtil.isNotEmpty(formula)) return 0;
  let exp = formula.replace("${", "").replace("}", "");
  let widgets = listFormulaWidgetNames(exp);
  widgets.forEach((name) => {
    let value = vars[name] || "0";
    exp = exp.replace(name, value);
  });
  let result = 0;
  try {
    result = eval(exp);
  } catch (error) {}
  // 最高4为精度
  return Math.round(result * Math.pow(10, 4)) / Math.pow(10, 4);
};

/**
 * 表单明细汇总计算
 *
 * @param {Array} detailValues
 * @param {String} formula
 */
export const formFormulaDetailCalc = (detailValues, formula) => {
  let detailWidgetNames = listFormulaWidgetNames(formula);
  if (!(detailWidgetNames && detailWidgetNames.length && detailValues && detailValues.length)) return "";
  let amount = 0;
  for (let detailValue of detailValues) {
    let formDetailVarContext = {};
    detailWidgetNames.forEach((detailWidgetName) => {
      formDetailVarContext[detailWidgetName] = detailValue[detailWidgetName] || 0;
    });
    amount += formulaEval(formula, formDetailVarContext) || 0;
  }
  return amount;
};

/**
 * 表单公式自动计算
 *
 * @param {Object} formValue
 * @param {Array} widgets
 */
export const formFormulaAutoCalc = (formValue, widgets) => {
  let formVarContext = {};
  widgets
    .filter((widget) => {
      let { name, type, formula, required, details: detailWidgets } = widget;
      if (required && [WIDGET.NUMBER, WIDGET.MONEY].includes(type)) {
        formVarContext[name] = formValue[name] || 0;
      } else if (type == WIDGET.DETAIL && detailWidgets && detailWidgets.length) {
        let detailValues = formValue[name] || [];
        for (let i = 0; i < detailValues.length; i++) {
          let formDetailVarContext = {};
          let detailValue = detailValues[i];
          detailWidgets
            .filter((detailWidget) => {
              let { name: detailName, type: detailType, formula: detailFormula, required: detailRequired } = detailWidget;
              if (detailRequired && [WIDGET.NUMBER, WIDGET.MONEY].includes(detailType)) {
                formDetailVarContext[detailName] = detailValue[detailName] || 0;
              }
              return detailType == WIDGET.FORMULA && detailFormula;
            })
            .forEach((detailWidget) => {
              // 处理公式
              let { name: detailName, formula: detailFormula } = detailWidget;
              let formualValue = formulaEval(detailFormula, formDetailVarContext) || 0;
              formDetailVarContext[detailName] = formualValue;
              detailValue[detailName] = formualValue;
            });

          let value = formVarContext[name] || 0;
          value += formulaEval(formula, formDetailVarContext) || 0;
          formVarContext[name] = value;
        }
      }
      return type == WIDGET.FORMULA && formula;
    })
    .forEach((widget) => {
      // 处理公式
      let { name, formula } = widget;
      let value = formulaEval(formula, formVarContext) || 0;
      formValue[name] = value;
    });
};


flow/common/FormAuth.js

import { NODE, WIDGET } from "@/components/flow/common/FlowConstant";
import { INITIATOR_VAR_NAME } from "./FormExp";

/**
 * 筛选出所有作为条件的组件
 *
 * @param {Object} startNode 流程开始节点
 * @param {Array} conditionWidgets 空的数组
 */
export function filterConditionWidgets(startNode, conditionWidgets) {
  let { childNode, conditionNodes } = startNode || {};
  if (childNode) filterConditionWidgets(childNode, conditionWidgets);
  (conditionNodes || []).forEach((conditionNode) => {
    if (conditionNode.childNode) filterConditionWidgets(conditionNode.childNode, conditionWidgets);
    (conditionNode.conditionGroups || []).forEach((conditionGroup) => {
      (conditionGroup.conditions || []).forEach((condition) => {
        let { varName } = condition;
        if (varName && varName !== INITIATOR_VAR_NAME) conditionWidgets.push(varName);
      });
    });
  });
}

/**
 * 根据名称筛选出组件
 *
 * @param {Array} widgets
 * @param {String} name
 * @returns widget
 */
const filterFormAuth = (widgets, name) => {
  let item = null;
  for (let i = 0; i < widgets.length; i++) {
    let widget = widgets[i];
    if (widget.type == WIDGET.DETAIL) {
      let details = widget.details || [];
      for (let ii = 0; ii < details.length; ii++) {
        let detail = details[ii];
        if (detail.name == name) return detail;
      }
    } else {
      if (widget.name == name) return widget;
    }
  }
  return item;
};

/**
 * 重新设置所有节点的表单权限
 *
 * @param {Object} startNode 流程开始节点
 * @param {Array} widgets 所有表单组件
 * @param {Array} conditionWidgets 条件节点使用的表单组件数组
 */
export function resetAllNodeFormAuth(startNode, widgets, conditionWidgets) {
  if (!startNode) startNode;
  let { childNode, conditionNodes, type } = startNode;
  if ([NODE.APPROVE, NODE.TRANSACT, NODE.COPY].includes(type)) {
    initNodeFormAuth(startNode, widgets, conditionWidgets);
  }
  if (childNode) resetAllNodeFormAuth(childNode, widgets, conditionWidgets);
  if (conditionNodes) conditionNodes.forEach((conditionNode) => resetAllNodeFormAuth(conditionNode, widgets, conditionWidgets));
}

/**
 * 初始化节点的标签权限
 * 表单选线写到节点的formAuths属性下面
 *
 * @param {Object} node 需要设置表单权限的节点
 * @param {Array} widgets 所有表单组件
 * @param {Array} conditionWidgets 条件节点使用的表单组件数组
 */
export function initNodeFormAuth(node, widgets, conditionWidgets) {
  let formAuths = node.formAuths;
  if (!!!formAuths) {
    formAuths = (widgets || []).map((widget) => {
      let { name, label, type } = widget;
      let formAuth;
      if (type == WIDGET.DETAIL) {
        formAuth = { name, type, label };
        formAuth.details = (widget.details || []).map((detail) => {
          return { name: detail.name, type: detail.type, label: detail.label, readable: true, editable: false };
        });
      } else {
        formAuth = { name, type, label, readable: true, editable: false };
      }
      return formAuth;
    });
  } else {
    formAuths = (widgets || []).map((widget) => {
      let { name, label, type } = widget;
      let formAuth;
      if (type == WIDGET.DETAIL) {
        formAuth = { name, type, label };
        formAuth.details = (widget.details || []).map((detail) => {
          let item = filterFormAuth(formAuths, detail.name);
          let readable = item ? item.readable : true;
          let editable = item ? item.editable : false;
          if (conditionWidgets.includes(detail.name)) editable = false;
          return { name: detail.name, type: detail.type, label: detail.label, readable, editable };
        });
      } else {
        let item = filterFormAuth(formAuths, name);
        let readable = item ? item.readable : true;
        let editable = item ? item.editable : false;
        if (conditionWidgets.includes(name)) editable = false;
        formAuth = { name, type, label, readable, editable };
      }
      return formAuth;
    });
  }
  node.formAuths = formAuths;
}

flow/common/FormExp.js

import { WIDGET } from "@/components/flow/common/FlowConstant";
import { useOrganStore } from "@/store/organ";
import ArrayUtil from "./ArrayUtil";
import ObjectUtil from "./ObjectUtil";

// 上面三个参数一一对应
export const operators = [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 10, 11, 12, 13, 14, 15, 20, 21];
export const names = {
  0: "等于",
  1: "不等于",
  2: "小于",
  3: "小于等于",
  4: "大于",
  5: "大于等于",
  10: "包含于",
  11: "不包含于",
  12: "等于",
  13: "不等于",
  14: "包含",
  15: "不包含",
  20: "属于",
  21: "不属于",
};
export const exps = {
  // 数值操作
  0: (v, t) => `${v}==${t}`,
  1: (v, t) => `${v}!=${t}`,
  2: (v, t) => `${v}<${t}`,
  3: (v, t) => `${v}<=${t}`,
  4: (v, t) => `${v}>${t}`,
  5: (v, t) => `${v}>=${t}`,
  // 字符串操作
  10: (v, t) => `fx.in0(${v},"${t}")`,
  11: (v, t) => `!fx.in0(${v},"${t}")`,
  12: (v, t) => `fx.eq0(${v},"${t}")`,
  13: (v, t) => `!fx.eq0(${v},"${t}")`,
  14: (v, t) => `fx.contain0(${v},"${t}")`,
  15: (v, t) => `!fx.contain0(${v},"${t}")`,
  // 数组操作
  20: (v, t) => {
    if (Array.isArray(t)) {
      let prams = t.map((v) => `"${v}"`).join(",");
      return `fx.has0(${v},${prams})`;
    } else {
      return `fx.has0(${v},"${t}")`;
    }
  },
  21: (v, t) => {
    if (Array.isArray(t)) {
      let prams = t.map((v) => `"${v}"`).join(",");
      return `!fx.has0(${v},${prams})`;
    } else {
      return `!fx.has0(${v},"${t}")`;
    }
  },
};

// 发起人变量名称
export const INITIATOR_VAR_NAME = "initiator";

const initiatorIn = (v, t) => {
  let prams = t.map((v) => `"${v}"`).join(",");
  return `fo.belong(businessKey,${v},${prams})`;
};

const initiatorNotIn = (v, t) => {
  let prams = t.map((v) => `"${v}"`).join(",");
  return `!fo.belong(businessKey,${v},${prams})`;
};

// 根据名称查询组件
const lookupWidget = (flowWidgets, name) => {
  if (flowWidgets && flowWidgets.length) {
    for (let flowWidget of flowWidgets) {
      if (flowWidget.name == name) return flowWidget;
      if (flowWidget.type == WIDGET.DETAIL) {
        for (let detail of flowWidget.details || []) {
          if (detail.name == name) return detail;
        }
      }
    }
  }
  return null;
};

// 获取组件名称
const lookupWidgetLabel = (flowWidget) => {
  return flowWidget ? flowWidget.label : "";
};

/**
 * 解析条件节点内容为可读文本
 */
export const showExpNodeContent = (branchNode, widgets = []) => {
  if (!branchNode.conditionGroups || branchNode.conditionGroups.length === 0) {
    return '';
  }

  const groupTexts = [];

  branchNode.conditionGroups.forEach((group, groupIdx) => {
    if (!group.conditions || group.conditions.length === 0) return;

    const conditionTexts = [];

    group.conditions.forEach((condition, idx) => {
      const { varName, operator, val } = condition;

      // 跳过无效条件
      if (!varName || operator === null || operator === undefined) return;

      // 获取字段标签
      let fieldLabel = varName;
      let fieldType = '';

      if (varName === INITIATOR_VAR_NAME) {
        fieldLabel = '发起人';
        fieldType = 'initiator';
      } else {
        const widget = widgets.find(w => w.name === varName);
        if (widget) {
          fieldLabel = widget.label || varName;
          fieldType = widget.type;
        }
      }

      // 获取操作符标签
      let operatorLabel = getOperatorLabel(operator);

      // 获取值文本
      let valueText = '';
      if (val !== null && val !== undefined && val !== '') {
        if (Array.isArray(val)) {
          if (varName === INITIATOR_VAR_NAME) {
            // 发起人ID转名称
            console.log(val);
            valueText = val.map(id => getById(id)?.name).join(", ");
          } else if (fieldType === WIDGET.DEPARTMENT) {
            // 部门ID转名称
            valueText = val.map(id => getDeptNameById(id)).join(', ');
          } else if (fieldType === WIDGET.EMPLOYEE) {
            // 员工ID转名称
            valueText = val.map(id => getById(id)?.name).join(", ");
          } else {
            valueText = val.join(', ');
          }
        } else {
          valueText = String(val);
        }
      }

      // 特殊处理"为空"和"不为空"操作符
      if (operator === 14) {
        conditionTexts.push(`${fieldLabel}为空`);
      } else if (operator === 15) {
        conditionTexts.push(`${fieldLabel}不为空`);
      } else if (operator === 20) {
        conditionTexts.push(`${fieldLabel}属于【${valueText}】`);
      } else if (operator === 21) {
        conditionTexts.push(`${fieldLabel}不属于【${valueText}】`);
      } else {
        conditionTexts.push(`${fieldLabel}${operatorLabel}${valueText ? '【' + valueText + '】' : ''}`);
      }
    });

    if (conditionTexts.length > 0) {
      const prefix = groupIdx === 0 ? '当' : '或';
      groupTexts.push(`${prefix}${conditionTexts.join('且')}`);
    }
  });

  return groupTexts.join('');
};

const { allRoles, allUsers, getById } = useOrganStore();

// 操作符标签映射
const operatorLabels = {
  0: "等于",
  1: "不等于",
  2: "大于",
  3: "大于等于",
  4: "小于",
  5: "小于等于",
  10: "包含",
  11: "不包含",
  12: "是",
  13: "不是",
  14: "为空",
  15: "不为空",
  20: "属于",
  21: "不属于",
};

// 获取操作符标签
const getOperatorLabel = (funIdx) => {
  return operatorLabels[funIdx] || FunNames[funIdx] || `操作${funIdx}`;
};

// 组装分支表达式
export const initBranchExp = (nodeConfig) => {
  recursiveBranchNode(nodeConfig);
};

// 遍历所有的分支节点
const recursiveBranchNode = (node) => {
  let { childNode, conditionNodes } = node || {};
  // 任务节点
  if (childNode) recursiveBranchNode(childNode);
  // 分支
  if (conditionNodes && conditionNodes.length > 0) {
    conditionNodes.forEach((conditionNode) => {
      let { childNode: childNode2, conditionNodes: conditionNodes2, conditionGroups } = conditionNode;
      if (childNode2) recursiveBranchNode(childNode2); // 任务节点
      if (conditionNodes2 && conditionNodes2.length > 0) conditionNodes2.forEach((conditionNode2) => recursiveBranchNode(conditionNode2));
      // 条件组
      if (conditionGroups && conditionGroups.length > 0) initExp(conditionNode);
    });
  }
};

// 构造分支条件表达式
export const initExp = (branchNode) => {
  let exp = branchNode.conditionGroups
    .map((conditionGroup) => {
      let { conditions } = conditionGroup;
      let subExp = conditions
        .filter((e) => ObjectUtil.isNotNull(e.varName) && ObjectUtil.isNotNull(e.operator) && ObjectUtil.isNotNull(e.val))
        .map((condition) => {
          let { varName, val, operator } = condition;
          let fun, newVal, segexp;
          if (varName === INITIATOR_VAR_NAME) {
            fun = operator == 20 ? initiatorIn : initiatorNotIn;
            newVal = val.map((i) => i);
            segexp = fun(varName, newVal);
          } else {
            fun = exps[operator];
            newVal = val;
            segexp = fun(varName, newVal);
          }
          console.log(fun, newVal, segexp);
          return segexp;
        })
        .join("&&");
      return `(${subExp})`;
    })
    .join("||");
  branchNode.conditionExpression = "${" + exp + "}";
};

// 可以作为条件的组件
const branchWidgets = [
  WIDGET.SINGLELINE_TEXT,
  WIDGET.NUMBER,
  WIDGET.MONEY,
  WIDGET.SINGLE_CHOICE,
  WIDGET.MULTI_CHOICE,
  WIDGET.DATE,
  WIDGET.DATE_RANGE,
  WIDGET.DEPARTMENT,
  WIDGET.EMPLOYEE,
  WIDGET.DETAIL,
  WIDGET.FORMULA,
];
// const branchDetailWidgets = [WIDGET.NUMBER, WIDGET.MONEY];

// 条件分支中，不可引用的组件需要被清除掉
export const cleanUnrequiredWidget = (flowWidgets, nodeConfig) => {
  let quotable = []; // 可被作为变量的组件
  (flowWidgets || []).forEach((flowWidget) => {
    let { type, required, details, formulaItems } = flowWidget;
    if ((required && branchWidgets.includes(type)) || WIDGET.FORMULA == type) {
      quotable.push(flowWidget);
    } else if (WIDGET.DETAIL == type && details && details.length && formulaItems && formulaItems.length) {
      quotable.push(flowWidget);
      // (flowWidget.details || []).forEach((detail) => {
      //   if (detail.required && branchDetailWidgets.includes(detail.type)) {
      //     quotable.push(detail);
      //   }
      // });
    }
  });
  quotable = quotable.map((i) => i.name);
  quotable.push(INITIATOR_VAR_NAME); // 添加固定的变量
  rmNotRequiredWidget(nodeConfig, quotable);
};

// 删除依赖非填项的分支条件
const rmNotRequiredWidget = (node, requireds) => {
  let { childNode, conditionNodes } = node || {};
  // 任务节点
  if (childNode) rmNotRequiredWidget(childNode, requireds);
  // 分支
  if (conditionNodes && conditionNodes.length > 0) {
    conditionNodes.forEach((conditionNode) => {
      let { childNode: childNode2, conditionNodes: conditionNodes2, conditionGroups } = conditionNode;
      if (childNode2) rmNotRequiredWidget(childNode2, requireds); // 任务节点
      if (conditionNodes2 && conditionNodes2.length > 0)
        conditionNodes2.forEach((conditionNode2) => rmNotRequiredWidget(conditionNode2, requireds));
      // 条件组
      if (conditionGroups && conditionGroups.length > 0) {
        let rmConditionGroupIds = [];
        conditionGroups.forEach((conditionGroup) => {
          let { conditions, id } = conditionGroup;
          let rmConditionVarNames = [];
          if (conditions && conditions.length > 0) {
            conditions.forEach((condition) => {
              let { varName } = condition;
              if (!requireds.includes(varName)) rmConditionVarNames.push(varName);
            });
          }

          // 单个条件
          if (rmConditionVarNames.length > 0) {
            rmConditionVarNames.forEach((varName) => {
              ArrayUtil.remove(conditions, "varName", varName);
            });
          }
          if (conditions.length == 0) rmConditionGroupIds.push(id);
        });

        // 删除空的条件组
        if (rmConditionGroupIds.length > 0) {
          rmConditionGroupIds.forEach((id) => {
            ArrayUtil.remove(conditionGroups, "id", id);
          });
        }
      }
    });
  }
};


flow/common/ObjectUtil.js

const toString = Object.prototype.toString;

// 对象复制
function copy(o) {
  return JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(o));
}

// 正在表达式检测值是否为数值
function isNumber(value) {
  var regrex = new RegExp("^(-?\\d+)(\\.\\d+)?$");
  return typeof value === "number" ? true : regrex.test(value);
}

// 检测是否为对象
function isObject(value) {
  return Object.getPrototypeOf(value) === Object.prototype;
}

function hyphenate(text) {
  return text.replace(/\B([A-Z])/g, "-$1").toLowerCase();
}

function isString(value) {
  return typeof value == "string";
}

function isArray(value) {
  return toString.call(value) === "[object Array]";
}

function isNotNull(value) {
  return value != null;
}

function isNotEmpty(value) {
  // 1. 排除 null/undefined
  if (value == null) return false;
  // 2. 排除空字符串
  if (typeof value === "string" && value.trim() === "") return false;
  // 3. 排除空数组
  if (Array.isArray(value) && value.length === 0) return false;
  // 4. 排除空对象
  if (typeof value === "object" && Object.keys(value).length === 0) return false;
  // 其他情况视为非空
  return true;
}

// 千分位
function comma(number) {
  if (number) {
    let values = (number + "").split(".");
    values[0] = values[0].replace(/\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, ",");
    return values.join(".");
  } else {
    return number;
  }
}

function limitScale(number, scale) {
  let text = String(number);
  if (text.includes(".")) {
    return text.substring(0, text.indexOf(".") + 1 + scale);
  }
  return number;
}

export default { copy, isNumber, isObject, isArray, hyphenate, isString, comma, limitScale, isNotNull, isNotEmpty };


flow/common/Snowflak.js

/**
 * A function for converting hex <-> dec w/o loss of precision.
 * By Dan Vanderkam http://www.danvk.org/hex2dec.html
 */

// Adds two arrays for the given base (10 or 16), returning the result.
// This turns out to be the only "primitive" operation we need.
function add(x, y, base) {
  var z = [];
  var n = Math.max(x.length, y.length);
  var carry = 0;
  var i = 0;
  while (i < n || carry) {
    var xi = i < x.length ? x[i] : 0;
    var yi = i < y.length ? y[i] : 0;
    var zi = carry + xi + yi;
    z.push(zi % base);
    carry = Math.floor(zi / base);
    i++;
  }
  return z;
}

// Returns a*x, where x is an array of decimal digits and a is an ordinary
// JavaScript number. base is the number base of the array x.
function multiplyByNumber(num, x, base) {
  if (num < 0) return null;
  if (num == 0) return [];

  var result = [];
  var power = x;
  while (true) {
    if (num & 1) {
      result = add(result, power, base);
    }
    num = num >> 1;
    if (num === 0) break;
    power = add(power, power, base);
  }

  return result;
}

function parseToDigitsArray(str, base) {
  var digits = str.split("");
  var ary = [];
  for (var i = digits.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    var n = parseInt(digits[i], base);
    if (isNaN(n)) return null;
    ary.push(n);
  }
  return ary;
}

function convertBase(str, fromBase, toBase) {
  var digits = parseToDigitsArray(str, fromBase);
  if (digits === null) return null;

  var outArray = [];
  var power = [1];
  for (var i = 0; i < digits.length; i++) {
    // invariant: at this point, fromBase^i = power
    if (digits[i]) {
      outArray = add(
        outArray,
        multiplyByNumber(digits[i], power, toBase),
        toBase
      );
    }
    power = multiplyByNumber(fromBase, power, toBase);
  }

  var out = "";
  for (var i = outArray.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    out += outArray[i].toString(toBase);
  }
  return out;
}

export function hexToDec(hexStr) {
  if (hexStr.substring(0, 2) === "0x") hexStr = hexStr.substring(2);
  hexStr = hexStr.toLowerCase();
  return convertBase(hexStr, 16, 10);
}

class Snowflake {
  constructor(options) {
    options = options || {};
    this.seq = 0;
    this.mid = (options.mid || 1) % 1023;// machine id
    this.offset = options.offset || 0;// 时间偏移量，当前时间减去该值，然后获取前42bits。有助于生成一个小的id。
    this.lastTime = 0;
  }

  generate() {
    const time = Date.now(),
      bTime = (time - this.offset).toString(2);

    // get the sequence number
    if (this.lastTime == time) {
      this.seq++;

      if (this.seq > 4095) {
        this.seq = 0;

        // make system wait till time is been shifted by one millisecond
        while (Date.now() <= time) { }
      }
    } else {
      this.seq = 0;
    }

    this.lastTime = time;

    let bSeq = this.seq.toString(2),
      bMid = this.mid.toString(2);

    // create sequence binary bit
    while (bSeq.length < 12) bSeq = "0" + bSeq;

    while (bMid.length < 10) bMid = "0" + bMid;

    const bid = bTime + bMid + bSeq;
    let id = "";

    for (let i = bid.length; i > 0; i -= 4) {
      id = parseInt(bid.substring(i - 4, i), 2).toString(16) + id;
    }

    return hexToDec(id);
  }
}

export default new Snowflake({
  mid: 0,
  offset: (2019 - 1970) * 31536000 * 1000,// 从1970开始计算
});



flow/dialog/FormSelector.vue

<template>
  <!-- 使用 ant-design-vue 的 Modal 组件，确保在单独的弹窗层显示 -->
  <a-modal
    :open="visible"
    :title="title"
    :width="isMobile ? '95%' : 700"
    :destroyOnClose="true"
    :maskClosable="false"
    :footer="null"
    @cancel="handleCancel"
    :bodyStyle="{ padding: isMobile ? '16px' : '24px' }"
    :centered="true"
  >
    <!-- 搜索区域 -->
    <div class="form-selector-search" :class="{ 'mobile-search': isMobile }">
      <a-input
        v-model:value="searchKey"
        placeholder="输入表单名称或编码搜索"
        allow-clear
        @pressEnter="handleSearch"
      >
        <template #prefix>
          <SearchOutlined />
        </template>
      </a-input>
      <a-checkbox v-model:checked="onlyUnbound" @change="handleSearch">
        仅显示未绑定流程的表单
      </a-checkbox>
    </div>

    <!-- 表单列表 -->
    <div class="form-selector-list" :class="{ 'mobile-list': isMobile }">
      <a-spin :spinning="loading" tip="加载中...">
        <template v-if="formList.length > 0">
          <div
            v-for="form in formList"
            :key="form.id"
            :class="[
              'form-item',
              {
                selected: selectedFormId === form.id,
                disabled: isFormDisabled(form),
                'mobile-item': isMobile,
              },
            ]"
            @click="handleSelect(form)"
          >
            <div class="form-item-left">
              <div class="form-icon">
                <FormOutlined />
              </div>
              <div class="form-info">
                <div class="form-name">
                  {{ form.formName }}
                  <span class="form-code">({{ form.formCode }})</span>
                </div>
                <div class="form-desc" v-if="form.description">
                  {{ truncateText(form.description, isMobile ? 30 : 50) }}
                </div>
                <div class="form-table" v-if="!isMobile && form.tableName">
                  数据表：{{ form.tableName }}
                </div>
                <div class="form-bound-tip" v-if="form.isBound">
                  <a-tag :color="isCurrentFlow(form) ? 'blue' : 'orange'" size="small">
                    {{ getBoundTip(form) }}
                  </a-tag>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div class="form-item-right">
              <div v-if="selectedFormId === form.id" class="selected-badge">
                <CheckOutlined />
                <span>已选择</span>
              </div>
              <a-button
                v-else-if="!isFormDisabled(form)"
                type="link"
                size="small"
                @click.stop="handleSelect(form)"
              >
                选择
              </a-button>
              <span v-else class="disabled-text">不可选</span>
            </div>
          </div>
        </template>

        <a-empty v-else :image="Empty.PRESENTED_IMAGE_SIMPLE">
          <template #description>
            <span>{{ emptyText }}</span>
          </template>
        </a-empty>
      </a-spin>
    </div>

    <!-- 底部按钮区域 -->
    <div class="form-selector-footer">
      <a-space>
        <a-button @click="handleCancel">取消</a-button>
        <a-button
          type="primary"
          :disabled="!selectedFormId"
          @click="handleConfirm"
          :loading="confirmLoading"
        >
          确认选择
        </a-button>
      </a-space>
    </div>
  </a-modal>
</template>

<script setup>
import { ref, watch, computed } from "vue";
import { SearchOutlined, FormOutlined, CheckOutlined } from "@ant-design/icons-vue";
import { Empty, message } from "ant-design-vue";
import BusinessFormApi from "@/api/biz/bizBusinessFormApi";

const props = defineProps({
  visible: {
    type: Boolean,
    default: false,
  },
  title: {
    type: String,
    default: "选择关联表单",
  },
  excludeFlowId: {
    type: String,
    default: null,
  },
  isMobile: {
    type: Boolean,
    default: false,
  },
});

const emit = defineEmits(["update:visible", "select"]);

// 状态管理
const loading = ref(false);
const confirmLoading = ref(false);
const formList = ref([]);
const searchKey = ref("");
const onlyUnbound = ref(true);
const selectedFormId = ref(null);
const selectedForm = ref(null);

// 空状态提示
const emptyText = computed(() => {
  if (onlyUnbound.value) {
    return "当前没有未绑定流程的表单";
  }
  return "暂无表单数据";
});

// 判断表单是否禁用
const isFormDisabled = (form) => {
  return form.isBound && form.flowDefId && form.flowDefId !== props.excludeFlowId;
};

// 判断是否为当前流程绑定的表单
const isCurrentFlow = (form) => {
  return form.isBound && form.flowDefId === props.excludeFlowId;
};

// 获取绑定提示文本
const getBoundTip = (form) => {
  if (form.flowDefId === props.excludeFlowId) {
    return "当前流程已绑定";
  }
  return `已绑定: ${form.flowName || "其他流程"}`;
};

// 截断文本
const truncateText = (text, length) => {
  if (!text) return "";
  return text.length > length ? text.slice(0, length) + "..." : text;
};

// 加载表单列表
const loadFormList = async () => {
  loading.value = true;
  try {
    const params = {
      SearchKey: searchKey.value || undefined,
      OnlyUnbound: onlyUnbound.value,
      ExcludeFlowId: props.excludeFlowId || undefined,
    };

    console.log("加载表单列表参数:", params);
    const response = await BusinessFormApi.getListForSelector(params);
    formList.value = Array.isArray(response) ? response : [];
    console.log("加载表单列表成功:", formList.value);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("加载表单列表失败:", error);
    message.error("加载表单列表失败");
    formList.value = [];
  } finally {
    loading.value = false;
  }
};

// 搜索处理
const handleSearch = () => {
  loadFormList();
};

// 选择表单
const handleSelect = (form) => {
  if (isFormDisabled(form)) {
    message.warning("该表单已绑定其他流程，请选择其他表单");
    return;
  }

  if (selectedFormId.value === form.id) {
    // 点击已选中的表单，取消选中
    selectedFormId.value = null;
    selectedForm.value = null;
  } else {
    // 选中新表单
    selectedFormId.value = form.id;
    selectedForm.value = form;
  }
};

// 确认选择
const handleConfirm = async () => {
  if (!selectedForm.value) {
    message.warning("请选择一个表单");
    return;
  }

  confirmLoading.value = true;
  try {
    // 检查表单是否仍可用
    if (isFormDisabled(selectedForm.value)) {
      message.warning("该表单已被其他流程绑定，请重新选择");
      // 刷新列表
      await loadFormList();
      selectedFormId.value = null;
      selectedForm.value = null;
      return;
    }

    // 返回完整的表单数据给父组件
    const selectedData = {
      id: selectedForm.value.id,
      formName: selectedForm.value.formName,
      formCode: selectedForm.value.formCode,
      tableName: selectedForm.value.tableName,
      description: selectedForm.value.description,
      // 保留原始数据中的其他字段
      ...selectedForm.value,
    };

    console.log("确认选择表单:", selectedData);
    emit("select", selectedData);
    handleCancel();
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("确认选择失败:", error);
    message.error("操作失败，请重试");
  } finally {
    confirmLoading.value = false;
  }
};

// 取消
const handleCancel = () => {
  emit("update:visible", false);
  // 延迟重置状态，避免闪烁
  setTimeout(() => {
    selectedFormId.value = null;
    selectedForm.value = null;
    searchKey.value = "";
    onlyUnbound.value = true;
    formList.value = [];
  }, 300);
};

// 监听弹窗显示
watch(
  () => props.visible,
  (val) => {
    if (val) {
      loadFormList();
    }
  }
);

// 暴露方法
defineExpose({
  loadFormList,
});
</script>

<style lang="less" scoped>
// 确保弹窗在最上层
:deep(.ant-modal) {
  z-index: 1050;

  .ant-modal-content {
    border-radius: 12px;
    overflow: hidden;
  }

  .ant-modal-header {
    border-bottom: 1px solid #f0f0f0;
    padding: 16px 24px;

    .ant-modal-title {
      font-size: 16px;
      font-weight: 600;
      color: #1f2329;
    }
  }

  .ant-modal-body {
    padding: 24px;
  }
}

.form-selector-search {
  display: flex;
  justify-content: space-between;
  align-items: center;
  margin-bottom: 20px;
  gap: 16px;

flow/dialog/Formula.vue

<!-- 计算公式 -->
<template>
  <a-modal
    :open="visible"
    @ok="handleOk"
    @cancel="handleClose"
    :class="'flow-formula-modal'"
    :draggable="true"
    title="编辑计算公式"
  >
    <!-- 显示计算公式 -->
    <div class="calc-screen">
      <div class="calc-items">
        <span class="clac-item" v-for="e in items" :key="e">{{ e.name }}</span>
      </div>
      <div class="calc-option">
        <div class="opt-btn" @click="handleBackClicked()"><left-outlined />退格</div>
        <div class="opt-btn" @click="handleClearClicked()">清空</div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- 计算公式选项 -->
    <div class="calc-options">
      <div class="item-box widgets-box">
        <div class="title">
          <a-tooltip title="仅必填的数字、金额控件用于计算">
            <info-circle-filled />
          </a-tooltip>
          控件：
        </div>
        <div class="item-wrapper">
          <a-button
            shape="round"
            class="widget-btn"
            v-for="widget in widgets"
            :key="widget"
            @click="handleWidgetClicked(widget)"
          >
            {{ widget.label }}
          </a-button>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="item-box symbols-container">
        <div class="title">符号：</div>
        <div class="item-wrapper">
          <a-button
            shape="round"
            v-for="symbol in symbols"
            :key="symbol"
            @click="handleItemClicked(symbol)"
          >
            <template #icon>{{ symbol.name }}</template>
          </a-button>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="item-box numbers-container">
        <div class="title">数字：</div>
        <div class="item-wrapper">
          <a-button
            shape="round"
            v-for="number in numbers"
            :key="number"
            @click="handleItemClicked(number)"
          >
            <template #icon>{{ number.name }}</template>
          </a-button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </a-modal>
  <div class="formula"></div>
</template>

<script setup>
import ObjectUtil from "@/components/flow/common/ObjectUtil";
import { isNumber } from "@/utils/is";
import { message } from "ant-design-vue";
import { LeftOutlined, InfoCircleFilled } from "@ant-design/icons-vue";
import { ref, watch } from "vue";

let props = defineProps({
  visible: { type: Boolean, default: false },
  widgets: { type: Array, default: [] }, // 所有组件
  formulaItems: { type: Array, default: [] }, // 公式元素
});
let emits = defineEmits(["update:visible", "ok"]);

// 流程定义对象
// let { flowDefinition } = useFlowStore();

const symbols = ref([
  { name: "+", value: "+" },
  { name: "-", value: "-" },
  { name: "×", value: "*" },
  { name: "÷", value: "/" },
  { name: "(", value: "(" },
  { name: ")", value: ")" },
  { name: ".", value: "." },
]);

const numbers = ref([
  { name: "0", value: "0" },
  { name: "1", value: "1" },
  { name: "2", value: "2" },
  { name: "3", value: "3" },
  { name: "4", value: "4" },
  { name: "5", value: "5" },
  { name: "6", value: "6" },
  { name: "7", value: "7" },
  { name: "8", value: "8" },
  { name: "9", value: "9" },
]);

// 选中的元素
const items = ref([]);
const handleItemClicked = (item) => {
  items.value.push(item);
};
const handleWidgetClicked = (widget) => {
  items.value.push({ name: widget.label, value: widget.name });
};
const handleBackClicked = () => {
  items.value.pop();
};
const handleClearClicked = () => {
  items.value = [];
};

// 校验计算公式格式是否正确
const formulaVerify = (widgets, elements) => {
  let widgetNames = widgets.map((item) => item.name);
  let exp = elements
    .map((item) => {
      let { value } = item;
      return widgetNames.includes(value) ? "1.0" : value;
    })
    .join("");

  let verified = true;
  try {
    if (exp) {
      let result = eval(exp);
      verified = result != Infinity && isNumber(result);
    }
  } catch (e) {
    verified = false;
  }
  return verified;
};

// 监听表单所有的组件变更，
// watch(flowDefinition.flowWidgets, (newVal) => {});

watch(
  () => props.visible,
  (isOpen) => {
    if (isOpen) {
      items.value = ObjectUtil.copy(props.formulaItems || []);
    }
  }
);

watch(
  () => props.widgets,
  (newVal) => {
    console.log("newVal", newVal);
  }
);

// 弹窗按钮
const handleOk = () => {
  let verified = formulaVerify(props.widgets, items.value);
  if (verified) {
    emits("ok", ObjectUtil.copy(items.value));
    handleClose();
  } else {
    message.error(`算数表达式格式有误！`);
  }
};
const handleClose = () => {
  emits("update:visible", false);
};
</script>

    .calc-items {

flow/dialog/OrganChooseBox.vue

<template>
  <a-modal
    v-if="isOpened"
    v-model:open="isOpened"
    @ok="onOkClicked()"
    @cancel="onCancelClicked()"
    :alignCenter="false"
    :width="modalWidth"
    :fullscreen="isMobile"
  >
    <template #title> 请选择用户 </template>
    <div class="user-content-wrap" :class="{ 'mobile-view': isMobile }">
      <div class="user-main-content">
        <!-- 左侧选择区域 -->
        <div class="picker-left" :class="{ 'mobile-full': isMobile }">
          <!-- 搜索框 -->
          <div class="search-container">
            <a-input
              v-model:value="keyword"
              placeholder="输入用户名称"
              allow-clear
              :maxlength="16"
              :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
            >
              <template #prefix
                ><search-outlined :style="{ fontSize: isMobile ? '20px' : '18px' }"
              /></template>
            </a-input>
          </div>

          <!-- 用户列表 -->
          <div class="picker-content">
            <div class="checkbox-list">
              <a-checkbox
                v-for="user in filteredUsers"
                :key="user.id"
                :value="user.id"
                :checked="user.checked"
                @change="onUserSelected($event.target.checked, user)"
              >
                <span class="checkbox-label">{{ user.name }}</span>
              </a-checkbox>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- 右侧已选区域（桌面端） -->
        <div v-if="!isMobile" class="picker-right">
          <div class="selected-header">
            <div class="selected-title">已选择 ({{ selectedUsers.length }})</div>
            <a-button
              v-if="selectedUsers.length > 0"
              type="text"
              size="small"
              @click="clearAll"
            >
              清空
            </a-button>
          </div>
          <div class="selected-items-box">
            <div class="selected-item" v-for="user in selectedUsers" :key="user.id">
              <div class="text">{{ user.name }}</div>
              <div class="delete-btn">
                <a @click="removeUser(user)">
                  <close-outlined :style="{ fontSize: '12px' }" />
                </a>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div v-if="selectedUsers.length === 0" class="empty-selected">暂无选择</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <!-- 移动端已选区域（底部固定） -->
      <div v-if="isMobile" class="mobile-selected-container">
        <div class="mobile-selected-header">
          <span>已选择 {{ selectedUsers.length }} 项</span>
          <a-button
            v-if="selectedUsers.length > 0"
            type="text"
            size="small"
            @click="clearAll"
          >
            清空
          </a-button>
        </div>
        <div class="mobile-selected-items">
          <div
            class="mobile-selected-tag"
            v-for="user in selectedUsers.slice(0, 5)"
            :key="user.id"
          >
            <a-tag closable size="small" @close="removeUser(user)" class="selected-tag">
              {{ user.name }}
            </a-tag>
          </div>
          <div v-if="selectedUsers.length > 5" class="more-items">
            还有 {{ selectedUsers.length - 5 }} 项...
          </div>
          <div v-if="selectedUsers.length === 0" class="empty-mobile-selected">
            暂无选择
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- 移动端操作按钮 -->
    <template v-if="isMobile" #footer>
      <div class="mobile-footer">
        <a-button @click="onCancelClicked" class="mobile-cancel-btn"> 取消 </a-button>
        <a-button type="primary" @click="onOkClicked" class="mobile-ok-btn">
          确定
        </a-button>
      </div>
    </template>
  </a-modal>
</template>

<script setup>
import { CloseOutlined, SearchOutlined } from "@ant-design/icons-vue";
import { computed, ref, watch, onMounted, onUnmounted } from "vue";
import tool from "@/utils/tool";

const props = defineProps({
  visible: { type: Boolean, default: false },
  selected: { type: Array, default: () => [] },
  onlyId: { type: Boolean, default: true },
});

const emit = defineEmits(["update:visible", "update:selected", "ok"]);

// 响应式屏幕尺寸检测
const isMobile = ref(false);
const modalWidth = ref(890);

const checkScreenSize = () => {
  const width = window.innerWidth;
  isMobile.value = width < 768;
  modalWidth.value = isMobile.value ? "100%" : 890;
};

const users = ref([]);
const keyword = ref("");
const selectedUsers = ref([]);

const isOpened = computed({
  get: () => props.visible,
  set: (val) => emit("update:visible", val),
});

// 从tool获取用户列表数据
const getUsers = () => {
  const userListData = tool.data.get("USER_LIST_DATA") || [];
  return JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(userListData));
};

// 筛选用户列表
const filteredUsers = computed(() => {
  if (!keyword.value) {
    return users.value;
  }
  return users.value.filter(
    (user) => user.name && user.name.toLowerCase().includes(keyword.value.toLowerCase())
  );
});

// 清空所有选择
const clearAll = () => {
  selectedUsers.value = [];
  users.value.forEach((user) => (user.checked = false));
};

// 初始化数据
const initSelected = () => {
  users.value = getUsers().map((user) => ({
    ...user,
    checked: false,
  }));

  // 重置已选列表
  selectedUsers.value = [];

  if (props.onlyId) {
    // 如果只传递ID，将选中的用户添加到已选列表
    props.selected.forEach((id) => {
      const user = users.value.find((u) => u.id === id);
      if (user) {
        user.checked = true;
        selectedUsers.value.push(user);
      }
    });
  } else {
    // 如果传递完整对象，处理对象格式
    props.selected.forEach((selectedItem) => {
      const user = users.value.find((u) => u.id === selectedItem.id);
      if (user) {
        user.checked = true;
        selectedUsers.value.push(user);
      }
    });
  }
};

// 监听窗口大小变化
onMounted(() => {
  checkScreenSize();
  window.addEventListener("resize", checkScreenSize);
});

onUnmounted(() => {
  window.removeEventListener("resize", checkScreenSize);
});

watch(
  () => props.visible,
  (newVal) => {
    if (newVal) {
      initSelected();
      checkScreenSize();
    }
  },
  { immediate: true }
);

// 用户选择事件
const onUserSelected = (checked, user) => {
  user.checked = checked;
  if (checked) {
    selectedUsers.value.push(user);
  } else {
    selectedUsers.value = selectedUsers.value.filter((u) => u.id !== user.id);
  }
};

// 移除用户
const removeUser = (user) => {
  selectedUsers.value = selectedUsers.value.filter((u) => u.id !== user.id);
  const userToUpdate = users.value.find((u) => u.id === user.id);
  if (userToUpdate) {
    userToUpdate.checked = false;
  }
};

// 确认选择
const onOkClicked = () => {
  let result;
  if (props.onlyId) {
    result = selectedUsers.value.map((user) => user.id);
  } else {
    result = selectedUsers.value.map((user) => ({
      id: user.id,
      type: 2, // 用户类型
      name: user.name,
    }));
  }

  isOpened.value = false;
  console.log(result);
  emit("update:selected", result);
  emit("ok", result);
};

// 取消
const onCancelClicked = () => {
  isOpened.value = false;
};
</script>

    }

    .mobile-cancel-btn {
      background: #f5f5f5;
      border: none;
    }
  }
}

// 移动端模态框样式优化
:deep(.ant-modal) {
  @media (max-width: 768px) {
    .ant-modal-header {
      padding: 16px;
      border-bottom: 1px solid #e4e5e7;
    }

    .ant-modal-body {
      padding: 0;
    }

    .ant-modal-footer {
      padding: 0;
    }
  }
}
</style>


flow/drawer/ApproverDrawer.vue

<template>
  <!-- 移动端全屏抽屉 -->
  <a-drawer
    :get-container="false"
    :width="isMobile ? '100%' : 540"
    :open="visible"
    :closable="!isMobile"
    :mask-closable="isMobile"
    :placement="isMobile ? 'bottom' : 'right'"
    :height="isMobile ? '85vh' : undefined"
    :class="['approver-drawer', { 'mobile-drawer': isMobile }]"
    :destroy-on-close="true"
    @close="handleCancel"
  >
    <!-- 移动端标题栏 - 只保留标题和返回按钮 -->
    <template #title v-if="isMobile">
      <div class="mobile-drawer-header">
        <div class="mobile-header-left">
          <a-button
            type="text"
            size="small"
            @click="handleCancel"
            class="mobile-close-btn"
          >
            <left-outlined />
          </a-button>
          <EditableText
            :value="flowNodeConfig.name"
            @change="onNodeNameChange"
            class="mobile-title"
            :compact="true"
          />
        </div>
      </div>
    </template>

    <!-- 桌面端标题 -->
    <template #title v-else>
      <EditableText :value="flowNodeConfig.name" @change="onNodeNameChange" />
    </template>

    <div class="approver-drawer__content" :class="{ 'mobile-content': isMobile }">
      <!-- 节点审批类型 -->
      <div class="approval-editor-node-type-wrapper">
        <div class="item-key-wrapper">
          <div class="item-key">审批类型</div>
        </div>
        <div class="item-content">
          <a-radio-group
            v-model:value="flowNodeConfig.approvalType"
            :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
          >
            <a-radio :value="0" class="radio-item">人工审批</a-radio>
            <a-radio :value="1" class="radio-item">自动通过</a-radio>
            <a-radio :value="2" class="radio-item">自动拒绝</a-radio>
          </a-radio-group>
        </div>
      </div>

      <!-- 审批人选择界面 -->
      <div class="approval-editor-tab-wrapper" v-if="flowNodeConfig.approvalType == 0">
        <!-- 移动端标签切换 -->
        <div class="mobile-tab-header" v-if="isMobile">
          <div
            v-for="tab in mobileTabs"
            :key="tab.value"
            :class="['mobile-tab-item', { active: viewEditorType === tab.value }]"
            @click="viewEditorType = tab.value"
          >
            <span>{{ tab.label }}</span>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- 桌面端标签切换 -->
        <a-radio-group
          v-model:value="viewEditorType"
          button-style="solid"
          size="large"
          class="desktop-tab-group"
          v-else
        >
          <a-radio-button :value="0">设置审批人</a-radio-button>
          <a-radio-button :value="1">操作权限</a-radio-button>
        </a-radio-group>

        <!-- 设置审批人 -->
        <div class="item-content-editor" v-if="viewEditorType == 0">
          <div class="content-wrap">
            <div class="item-content">
              <!-- 审批人列表 -->
              <div class="item-wrap approver">
                <div
                  class="approver-list"
                  v-if="flowNodeConfig.assignees && flowNodeConfig.assignees.length > 0"
                >
                  <div
                    class="approver-wrapper"
                    v-for="(item, idx) in flowNodeConfig.assignees"
                    :key="item.rid"
                  >
                    <div class="header">
                      <span class="header-title">审批人{{ idx + 1 }}</span>
                      <delete-outlined
                        class="delete-icon"
                        :style="{ fontSize: isMobile ? '16px' : '18px' }"
                        @click="delApprover(item)"
                        v-if="flowNodeConfig.assignees.length > 1"
                      />
                    </div>
                    <div class="main-content">
                      <a-radio-group
                        class="radio-group"
                        v-model:value="item.assigneeType"
                        @change="onAssigneeTypeChanged(item)"
                        :size="isMobile ? 'small' : 'middle'"
                      >
                        <a-row :gutter="[8, 8]">
                          <a-col
                            v-for="option in assigneeOptions"
                            :key="option.value"
                            :span="isMobile ? 12 : 8"
                          >
                            <a-radio
                              :value="option.value"
                              :disabled="option.disabled && haveMultiNode"
                              class="assignee-radio"
                            >
                              <span class="radio-label">{{ option.label }}</span>
                            </a-radio>
                          </a-col>
                        </a-row>
                      </a-radio-group>
                    </div>
                    <div class="sub-content" v-if="![0, 7].includes(item.assigneeType)">
                      <div class="sub-content-top-line"></div>

                      <!-- 上级选择 -->
                      <template v-if="item.assigneeType == 1">
                        <p class="bold">请选择上级</p>
                        <div class="form-item-wrapper">
                          <div class="form-label">发起人的</div>
                          <a-select
                            placeholder="请选择上级"
                            v-model:value="item.layer"
                            :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                            :dropdown-class-name="
                              isMobile ? 'mobile-select-dropdown' : ''
                            "
                          >
                            <template #dropdownRender="{ menuNode }">
                              <div>
                                <div class="switch-container">
                                  <div class="select-tip">从直属上级向上选择</div>
                                  <a-button
                                    type="link"
                                    @click="switchLayerType(item)"
                                    class="switch-link"
                                    size="small"
                                  >
                                    <swap-outlined />
                                    {{
                                      item.layerType == 0
                                        ? "切为最高上级向下"
                                        : "切为直属上级向上"
                                    }}
                                  </a-button>
                                </div>
                                <a-divider style="margin: 8px 0" />
                                <!-- 最简单的方式：直接渲染 menuNode 组件 -->
                                <component :is="menuNode" />
                              </div>
                            </template>
                            <a-select-option v-for="i in 20" :value="i - 1" :key="i">
                              <template v-if="item.layerType == 0">
                                {{
                                  i == 1 ? "直属上级" : "直属上级加 " + (i - 1) + " 级"
                                }}
                              </template>
                              <template v-else>
                                {{
                                  i == 1 ? "最高上级" : "最高上级减 " + (i - 1) + " 级"
                                }}
                              </template>
                            </a-select-option>
                          </a-select>
                        </div>
                      </template>
                      <!-- 部门负责人选择 -->
                      <template v-else-if="item.assigneeType == 2">
                        <p class="bold">请选择部门负责人</p>
                        <div class="form-item-wrapper">
                          <div class="form-label">发起人的</div>
                          <a-select
                            placeholder="请选择部门负责人"
                            v-model:value="item.layer"
                            :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                            :dropdown-class-name="
                              isMobile ? 'mobile-select-dropdown' : ''
                            "
                          >
                            <template #dropdownRender="{ menuNode }">
                              <div>
                                <div class="switch-container">
                                  <div class="select-tip">从直属部门负责人向上选择</div>
                                  <a-button
                                    type="link"
                                    @click="switchLayerType(item)"
                                    class="switch-link"
                                    size="small"
                                  >
                                    <swap-outlined />
                                    {{
                                      item.layerType == 0
                                        ? "切为最高部门向下"
                                        : "切为直属部门向上"
                                    }}
                                  </a-button>
                                </div>
                                <a-divider style="margin: 8px 0" />
                                <!-- 最简单的方式：直接渲染 menuNode 组件 -->
                                <component :is="menuNode" />
                              </div>
                            </template>
                            <a-select-option v-for="i in 20" :value="i - 1" :key="i">
                              <template v-if="item.layerType == 0">
                                {{
                                  i == 1
                                    ? "直属部门负责人"
                                    : "直属部门负责人加 " + (i - 1) + " 级"
                                }}
                              </template>
                              <template v-else>
                                {{
                                  i == 1
                                    ? "最高部门负责人"
                                    : "最高部门负责人减 " + (i - 1) + " 级"
                                }}
                              </template>
                            </a-select-option>
                          </a-select>
                        </div>
                      </template>

                      <!-- 指定成员选择 -->
                      <template v-else-if="item.assigneeType == 4">
                        <p class="bold">
                          添加成员
                          <span class="hint-text">（不能超过 25 人）</span>
                        </p>
                        <div class="assignee-box">
                          <a-button
                            size="small"
                            @click="onAssigneeClick(item)"
                            :shape="isMobile ? 'circle' : 'default'"
                            class="add-member-btn"
                          >
                            <plus-outlined />
                          </a-button>
                          <div class="assignee-list">
                            <a-tag
                              v-for="userId in item.assignees"
                              :key="userId"
                              :size="isMobile ? 'small' : 'middle'"
                              closable
                              @close="removeAssignee(item, userId)"
                              class="member-tag"
                            >
                              {{ getUserById(userId)?.name }}
                            </a-tag>
                            <div
                              v-if="!item.assignees || item.assignees.length === 0"
                              class="empty-hint"
                            >
                              点击上方按钮添加成员
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </template>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>

                <!-- 空状态 -->
                <div class="empty-state" v-else>
                  <div class="empty-icon">
                    <team-outlined />
                  </div>
                  <div class="empty-text">暂未设置审批人</div>
                  <div class="empty-hint">点击下方按钮添加审批人</div>
                </div>

                <!-- 添加审核人按钮 -->
                <div class="add-operator" v-if="!onlyOneNode">
                  <a-button
                    type="dashed"
                    @click="addApprover"
                    :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                    :block="isMobile"
                    class="add-approver-btn"
                  >
                    <template #icon>
                      <plus-outlined />
                    </template>
                    {{
                      flowNodeConfig.assignees && flowNodeConfig.assignees.length > 0
                        ? "继续添加审批人"
                        : "添加审批人"
                    }}
                  </a-button>
                </div>
              </div>

              <!-- 会签、或签、序签 -->
              <div
                class="item-wrap sign-type"
                v-if="haveMultiNode || isInitiatorChoiceOrAssignee"
              >
                <div class="item-key-wrapper">
                  <div class="item-key">多人审批时采用的审批方式</div>
                </div>
                <div class="item-content">
                  <a-radio-group
                    v-model:value="flowNodeConfig.multiInstanceApprovalType"
                    :size="isMobile ? 'small' : 'middle'"
                  >
                    <div style="margin-bottom: 12px">
                      <a-radio :value="1" class="multi-radio-item">
                        会签（需所有审批人同意）
                      </a-radio>
                    </div>
                    <div style="margin-bottom: 12px">
                      <a-radio :value="2" class="multi-radio-item">
                        或签（一名审批人同意即可）
                      </a-radio>
                    </div>
                    <div v-if="isSameAssigneeType && !isInitiatorChoiceOrAssignee">
                      <a-radio :value="3" class="multi-radio-item">
                        依次审批（按顺序依次审批）
                      </a-radio>
                    </div>
                  </a-radio-group>
                </div>
              </div>

              <!-- 审批人为空时 -->
              <div class="item-wrap approver-null">
                <div class="item-key-wrapper">
                  <div class="item-key">审批人为空时</div>
                </div>
                <div class="item-content">
                  <a-radio-group
                    v-model:value="flowNodeConfig.flowNodeNoAuditorType"
                    @change="onNoAuditorTypeChanged"
                    :size="isMobile ? 'small' : 'middle'"
                  >
                    <div style="margin-bottom: 12px">
                      <a-radio :value="0" class="null-radio-item">自动通过</a-radio>
                    </div>
                    <div style="margin-bottom: 12px">
                      <a-radio :value="1" class="null-radio-item">指定人员审批</a-radio>
                    </div>
                  </a-radio-group>

                  <div
                    class="approver-null-select-box"
                    v-if="flowNodeConfig.flowNodeNoAuditorType !== 0"
                  >
                    <div class="form-item-wrapper">
                      <!-- 指定成员选择器 -->
                      <a-select
                        v-if="flowNodeConfig.flowNodeNoAuditorType == 1"
                        placeholder="请选择成员"
                        v-model:value="flowNodeConfig.flowNodeNoAuditorAssignee"
                        :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                        style="width: 100%"
                        allow-clear
                        :dropdown-class-name="isMobile ? 'mobile-select-dropdown' : ''"
                      >
                        <a-select-option
                          v-for="user in allUsers"
                          :key="user.id"
                          :value="user.id"
                        >
                          {{ user.name }}
                        </a-select-option>
                      </a-select>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>

              <!-- 审批人与提交人为同一人时 -->
              <div class="item-wrap approver-self">
                <div class="item-key-wrapper">
                  <div class="item-key">审批人与提交人为同一人时</div>
                </div>
                <div class="item-content">
                  <a-radio-group
                    v-model:value="flowNodeConfig.flowNodeSelfAuditorType"
                    :size="isMobile ? 'small' : 'middle'"
                  >
                    <div style="margin-bottom: 12px">
                      <a-radio :value="0" class="self-radio-item"
                        >由发起人对自己审批</a-radio
                      >
                    </div>
                    <div style="margin-bottom: 12px">
                      <a-radio :value="1" class="self-radio-item">自动跳过</a-radio>
                    </div>
                    <div style="margin-bottom: 12px">
                      <a-radio :value="2" class="self-radio-item"
                        >转交给直接上级审批</a-radio
                      >
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <a-radio :value="3" class="self-radio-item"
                        >转交给部门负责人审批</a-radio
                      >
                    </div>
                  </a-radio-group>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- 设置操作权限 -->
        <div class="item-content-auth" v-else-if="viewEditorType == 1">
          <div class="content-wrap">
            <div class="item-content">
              <div class="item-wrap auth-list">
                <a-checkbox-group
                  v-model:value="authValues"
                  :size="isMobile ? 'small' : 'middle'"
                >
                  <div style="margin-bottom: 12px">
                    <a-checkbox class="auth-item" :value="1"> 允许转交 </a-checkbox>
                  </div>
                  <div style="margin-bottom: 12px">
                    <a-checkbox class="auth-item" :value="2">
                      允许加签 / 减签
                    </a-checkbox>
                  </div>
                  <div style="margin-bottom: 12px">
                    <a-checkbox class="auth-item" :value="3"> 允许回退 </a-checkbox>
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <a-checkbox class="auth-item" :value="4"> 允许编辑 </a-checkbox>
                  </div>
                </a-checkbox-group>
              </div>
              <div class="item-wrap tip">
                <div class="item-key-wrapper">
                  <div class="item-key">提示：</div>
                </div>
                <div class="more-info">
                  <p>
                    若审批人设置为连续多级上级、连续多级部门负责人时，允许的加签 /
                    减签不能生效。
                  </p>
                  <p>若多人审批方式为依次审批时，允许的加签 / 减签不能生效。</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- 底部按钮 - 桌面端和移动端统一放在底部 -->
    <template #footer>
      <div class="drawer-footer" :class="{ 'mobile-footer': isMobile }">
        <a-button @click="handleCancel" :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'">
          取消
        </a-button>
        <a-button
          type="primary"
          @click="saveApprover"
          :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
        >
          保存
        </a-button>
      </div>
    </template>

    <!-- 成员选择对话框 -->
    <OrganChooseBox
      v-if="showChooseAssignee"
      :visible="showChooseAssignee"
      :selected="selectedAssignee.assignees || []"
      :hidden-dept="true"
      :hidden-role="true"
      :is-mobile="isMobile"
      title="选择审批人"
      @update:visible="(val) => (showChooseAssignee = val)"
      @update:selected="selectedAssigneeChange"
    />
  </a-drawer>
</template>

<script setup>
import EditableText from "@/components/common/EditableText.vue";
import { useOrganStore } from "@/store/organ";
import { useFlowStore } from "@/store/flow";
import {
  DeleteOutlined,
  PlusOutlined,
  QuestionCircleOutlined,
  SwapOutlined,
  LeftOutlined,
  TeamOutlined,
} from "@ant-design/icons-vue";
import { computed, onMounted, ref, toRaw, watch, onUnmounted } from "vue";
import ArrayUtil from "../common/ArrayUtil";
import Snowflake from "../common/Snowflake";
import OrganChooseBox from "../dialog/OrganChooseBox.vue";
import NodeFormAuthSetting from "../NodeFormAuthSetting.vue";

const flowStore = useFlowStore();
const selectedAssigneeChange = (val) => {
  if (selectedAssignee.value) {
    toRaw(selectedAssignee.value).assignees = val;
  }
};
const { allUsers, getUserById } = useOrganStore();
const { showApproverDrawer, setApproverConfig } = flowStore;
const isApproverDrawerOpened = computed(() => flowStore.isApproverDrawerOpened);
const approverConfig0 = computed(() => flowStore.approverConfig0);
const workFlowDef = computed(() => flowStore.flowDefinition?.workFlowDef || {});

// 检测是否为移动端
const isMobile = ref(false);

const checkMobile = () => {
  isMobile.value = window.innerWidth <= 768;
};

onMounted(() => {
  checkMobile();
  window.addEventListener("resize", checkMobile);
});

onUnmounted(() => {
  window.removeEventListener("resize", checkMobile);
});

const visible = computed({
  get: () => isApproverDrawerOpened.value,
  set: (val) => {
    if (!val) close();
  },
});

const viewEditorType = ref(0);
const _uid = ref(0);
const flowNodeConfig = ref({
  name: "审批人",
  assignees: [],
  approvalType: 0,
  multiInstanceApprovalType: 0,
  flowNodeNoAuditorType: 0,
  flowNodeSelfAuditorType: 0,
  assignable: 0,
  signable: 0,
  backable: 0,
});

// 移动端标签配置
const mobileTabs = ref([
  { label: "审批人", value: 0 },
  { label: "操作权限", value: 1 },
]);

// 审批人选项配置
const assigneeOptions = computed(() => [
  { label: "发起人本人", value: 0 },
  { label: "上级", value: 1 },
  { label: "部门负责人", value: 2 },
  { label: "指定成员", value: 4 },
  { label: "发起人自选", value: 7, disabled: true },
]);

// 权限值计算属性
const authValues = computed({
  get: () => {
    const values = [];
    if (flowNodeConfig.value.assignable) values.push(1);
    if (flowNodeConfig.value.signable) values.push(2);
    if (flowNodeConfig.value.backable) values.push(3);
    if (flowNodeConfig.value.signature === 0) values.push(4);
    return values;
  },
  set: (values) => {
    flowNodeConfig.value.assignable = values.includes(1) ? 1 : 0;
    flowNodeConfig.value.signable = values.includes(2) ? 1 : 0;
    flowNodeConfig.value.backable = values.includes(3) ? 1 : 0;
    flowNodeConfig.value.signature = values.includes(4) ? 0 : undefined;
  },
});

// 是否为单个审批人节点
const onlyOneNode = computed(() => {
  const firstAssigneeType = flowNodeConfig.value.assignees?.[0]?.assigneeType;
  return [7].includes(firstAssigneeType);
});

// 是否含有多个审批人
const haveMultiNode = computed(() => {
  return flowNodeConfig.value.assignees?.length > 1;
});

// 是否设置了发起人自选或指定审批人
const isInitiatorChoiceOrAssignee = computed(() => {
  const firstAssigneeType = flowNodeConfig.value.assignees?.[0]?.assigneeType;
  return [4, 7].includes(firstAssigneeType);
});

// 多个审核人设置的类型是否一致
const isSameAssigneeType = computed(() => {
  if (!flowNodeConfig.value.assignees || flowNodeConfig.value.assignees.length === 1)
    return false;

  const firstType = flowNodeConfig.value.assignees[0].assigneeType;
  const allSame = flowNodeConfig.value.assignees.every(
    (item) => item.assigneeType === firstType
  );

  // 如果不能使用序签，则默认会签
  if (!allSame && flowNodeConfig.value.multiInstanceApprovalType === 3) {
    flowNodeConfig.value.multiInstanceApprovalType = 1;
  }

  return allSame;
});

// 审批人选择指定成员
const showChooseAssignee = ref(false);
const selectedAssignee = ref(null);

const onAssigneeClick = (item) => {
  // 确保 assignees 数组存在
  if (!item.assignees) {
    item.assignees = [];
  }
  // 存储当前操作的审批人项的引用
  selectedAssignee.value = item;
  showChooseAssignee.value = true;
};

// 移除指定成员
const removeAssignee = (item, userId) => {
  if (item.assignees) {
    const index = item.assignees.indexOf(userId);
    if (index > -1) {
      item.assignees.splice(index, 1);
    }
  }
};

watch(
  approverConfig0,
  (val) => {
    if (val?.value) {
      flowNodeConfig.value = {
        ...flowNodeConfig.value,
        ...val.value,
      };
      viewEditorType.value = 0;
      _uid.value = val.id;

      // 确保assignees数组存在
      if (!flowNodeConfig.value.assignees) {
        flowNodeConfig.value.assignees = [];
      }
    }
  },
  { immediate: true, deep: true }
);

watch(
  () => flowNodeConfig.value.assignees,
  (newAssignees) => {
    if (!newAssignees || newAssignees.length === 0) return;

    const firstAssigneeType = newAssignees[0]?.assigneeType;

    if (newAssignees.length === 1) {
      // 只设置了一个审批人
      if ([7].includes(firstAssigneeType)) {
        flowNodeConfig.value.multiInstanceApprovalType = 3;
      }

      if (
        [4, 7].includes(firstAssigneeType) &&
        [0, 3].includes(flowNodeConfig.value.multiInstanceApprovalType)
      ) {
        if (flowNodeConfig.value.multiInstanceApprovalType === 0) {
          flowNodeConfig.value.multiInstanceApprovalType = 1;
        }
      }
    } else {
      // 如果设置了多个审批人，默认会签
      if (
        !flowNodeConfig.value.multiInstanceApprovalType ||
        flowNodeConfig.value.multiInstanceApprovalType === 0
      ) {
        flowNodeConfig.value.multiInstanceApprovalType = 1;
      }
    }
  },
  { deep: true }
);

// 切换上级和部门负责人的人事层级关系
const switchLayerType = (assignee) => {
  assignee.layerType = assignee.layerType === 0 ? 1 : 0;
};

// 审批人类型切换时
const onAssigneeTypeChanged = (assignee) => {
  const { assigneeType } = assignee;

  // 重置相关字段
  const fieldsToDelete = ["layerType", "layer", "assignees"];

  fieldsToDelete.forEach((field) => {
    if (field in assignee) {
      delete assignee[field];
    }
  });

  // 根据类型设置默认值
  if ([1, 2].includes(assigneeType)) {
    assignee.layerType = 0;
    assignee.layer = 0;
  } else if ([4].includes(assigneeType)) {
    assignee.assignees = [];
  }
};

// 节点审批人为空选项改变时
const onNoAuditorTypeChanged = () => {
  if (flowNodeConfig.value.flowNodeNoAuditorType === 1) {
    delete flowNodeConfig.value.flowNodeAuditAdmin;
  } else if (flowNodeConfig.value.flowNodeNoAuditorType === 2) {
    delete flowNodeConfig.value.flowNodeNoAuditorAssignee;
  } else {
    delete flowNodeConfig.value.flowNodeNoAuditorAssignee;
    delete flowNodeConfig.value.flowNodeAuditAdmin;
  }
};

// 添加审批人
const addApprover = () => {
  if (!flowNodeConfig.value.assignees) {
    flowNodeConfig.value.assignees = [];
  }
  flowNodeConfig.value.assignees.push({
    rid: Snowflake.generate(),
    assigneeType: 0,
  });
};

// 删除审批人
const delApprover = (approver) => {
  ArrayUtil.remove(flowNodeConfig.value.assignees, "rid", approver.rid);

  // 当设置的审批人删除到一个时，节点类型重置
  if (flowNodeConfig.value.assignees.length === 1) {
    flowNodeConfig.value.multiInstanceApprovalType = 0;
  }
};

// 编辑节点名称
const onNodeNameChange = (name) => {
  flowNodeConfig.value.name = name;
  saveApprover(false);
};

// 取消处理
const handleCancel = () => {
  close();
};

// 保存
const saveApprover = (leave = true) => {
  // 保存当前配置
  const savedConfig = toRaw(flowNodeConfig.value);

  // 确保每个指定成员的 assignees 字段是数组
  if (savedConfig.assignees) {
    savedConfig.assignees.forEach((assignee) => {
      if (assignee.assigneeType === 4 && !Array.isArray(assignee.assignees)) {
        assignee.assignees = [];
      }
    });
  }

  // 如果有原有配置，保留 childNode
  if (approverConfig0.value?.value?.childNode) {
    savedConfig.childNode = approverConfig0.value.value.childNode;
  }

  setApproverConfig({
    value: savedConfig,
    flag: true,
    id: _uid.value,
  });
  leave && close();
};

const close = () => {
  showApproverDrawer(false);
};
</script>
