flow/drawer/ConditionDrawer.vue

<template>
  <!-- 移动端全屏抽屉 -->
  <a-drawer
    v-if="visible"
    :get-container="false"
    :width="isMobile ? '100%' : 540"
    :open="visible"
    :closable="!isMobile"
    :maskClosable="isMobile"
    :placement="isMobile ? 'bottom' : 'right'"
    :height="isMobile ? '90vh' : undefined"
    :class="['condition-drawer', { 'mobile-drawer': isMobile }]"
    :footer-style="{ textAlign: 'right' }"
    @close="handleCancel"
  >
    <!-- 桌面端标题 -->
    <template #title v-if="!isMobile">
      <EditableText :value="flowNodeConfig.name" @change="onNodeNameChange" />
    </template>

    <!-- 移动端标题栏 -->
    <template v-else #title>
      <div class="mobile-drawer-header">
        <div class="mobile-header-left">
          <a-button
            type="text"
            size="small"
            @click="handleCancel"
            class="mobile-close-btn"
          >
            <LeftOutlined />
          </a-button>
          <EditableText
            :value="flowNodeConfig.name"
            @change="onNodeNameChange"
            class="mobile-title"
            :compact="isMobile"
          />
        </div>
        <a-button
          type="primary"
          size="small"
          @click="saveCondition()"
          class="mobile-save-btn"
        >
          保存
        </a-button>
      </div>
    </template>

    <!-- 抽屉内容 -->
    <div class="condition-drawer__content" :class="{ 'mobile-content': isMobile }">
      <div class="top-tips">
        <InfoCircleOutlined v-if="isMobile" />
        满足以下条件时进入当前分支
      </div>

      <!-- 单个条件组编辑器 -->
      <div
        class="condition-groups-container"
        v-if="flowNodeConfig.conditionGroups && flowNodeConfig.conditionGroups.length > 0"
      >
        <template
          v-for="(conditionGroup, conditionGroupIdx) in flowNodeConfig.conditionGroups"
          :key="conditionGroup.id"
        >
          <!-- 或满足分隔线 -->
          <div v-if="conditionGroupIdx != 0" class="or-branch-link-tip">
            <div class="or-line"></div>
            <span class="or-text">或满足</span>
            <div class="or-line"></div>
          </div>

          <div
            class="condition-group-editor"
            :class="{ 'mobile-condition-group': isMobile }"
          >
            <div class="header">
              <div class="header-content">
                <div class="group-tag">条件组 {{ conditionGroupIdx + 1 }}</div>
                <DeleteOutlined
                  class="branch-delete-icon"
                  @click="rmConditionGroup(conditionGroup)"
                />
              </div>
            </div>

            <div class="main-content">
              <!-- 单个条件 - 修复v-if和v-for嵌套问题 -->
              <template
                v-for="(condition, idx) in conditionGroup.conditions"
                :key="condition.id"
              >
                <div class="condition-item">
                  <div class="condition-row">
                    <div class="condition-relation">
                      <span class="relation-text">{{ idx === 0 ? "当" : "且" }}</span>
                    </div>

                    <div class="condition-content-wrapper">
                      <!-- 字段选择 -->
                      <div class="condition-field">
                        <a-select
                          v-model:value="condition.varName"
                          @change="onConditionChange($event, condition)"
                          :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                          placeholder="选择字段"
                          :dropdownClassName="isMobile ? 'mobile-select-dropdown' : ''"
                          :style="{ width: isMobile ? '100%' : '160px' }"
                        >
                          <a-select-option
                            v-for="opt in conditionOptions"
                            :key="opt.name"
                            :value="opt.name"
                          >
                            <div class="option-content">
                              <div class="option-label">{{ opt.label }}</div>
                              <div v-if="isMobile" class="option-type">
                                {{ getOptionTypeLabel(opt.type) }}
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          </a-select-option>
                        </a-select>
                      </div>

                      <!-- 操作符选择 -->
                      <div v-if="condition.varName" class="condition-operator">
                        <a-select
                          v-model:value="condition.operator"
                          :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                          :style="{ width: isMobile ? '100%' : '120px' }"
                        >
                          <a-select-option
                            v-for="funIdx in condition.operators"
                            :key="funIdx"
                            :value="funIdx"
                          >
                            {{ getOperatorLabel(funIdx) }}
                          </a-select-option>
                        </a-select>
                      </div>

                      <!-- 条件值 -->
                      <div
                        v-if="
                          condition.operator !== null && condition.operator !== undefined
                        "
                        class="condition-value"
                      >
                        <!-- 发起人条件 -->
                        <template v-if="condition.varName === INITIATOR_VAR_NAME">
                          <div class="value-select initiator-select">
                            <div
                              class="selected-users"
                              @click="onOpenOrganChooseBox(condition)"
                            >
                              <template
                                v-if="
                                  Array.isArray(condition.val) && condition.val.length > 0
                                "
                              >
                                <div class="user-tags">
                                  <a-tag
                                    v-for="userId in condition.val.slice(
                                      0,
                                      isMobile ? 2 : 3
                                    )"
                                    :key="userId"
                                    :size="isMobile ? 'small' : 'middle'"
                                    closable
                                    @close="removeUser(condition, userId)"
                                    class="user-tag"
                                  >
                                    {{ getUserName(userId) }}
                                  </a-tag>
                                  <span
                                    v-if="condition.val.length > (isMobile ? 2 : 3)"
                                    class="more-count"
                                  >
                                    +{{ condition.val.length - (isMobile ? 2 : 3) }}
                                  </span>
                                </div>
                              </template>
                              <div v-else class="placeholder">点击选择人员</div>
                              <RightOutlined class="arrow-icon" />
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </template>

                        <!-- 表单组件条件 -->
                        <template v-else-if="condition.varName">
                          <div class="val-content">
                            <!-- 单行文本 -->
                            <div
                              v-if="
                                getWidget(condition.varName).type ===
                                WIDGET.SINGLELINE_TEXT
                              "
                            >
                              <a-input
                                v-model:value="condition.val"
                                :maxlength="64"
                                allow-clear
                                :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                                placeholder="请输入"
                              />
                            </div>

                            <!-- 数字、明细、公式 -->
                            <div
                              v-else-if="
                                [WIDGET.NUMBER, WIDGET.DETAIL, WIDGET.FORMULA].includes(
                                  getWidget(condition.varName).type
                                )
                              "
                            >
                              <a-input-number
                                v-model:value="condition.val"
                                :max="999999999999999"
                                :formatter="(v) => ObjectUtil.limitScale(v, 2)"
                                :controls="false"
                                :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                                placeholder="请输入"
                                style="width: 100%"
                              />
                            </div>

                            <!-- 金额 -->
                            <div
                              v-else-if="
                                [WIDGET.MONEY].includes(getWidget(condition.varName).type)
                              "
                            >
                              <a-input-number
                                v-model:value="condition.val"
                                :max="999999999999999"
                                :formatter="(v) => ObjectUtil.limitScale(v, 2)"
                                :controls="false"
                                :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                                placeholder="请输入"
                                style="width: 100%"
                              >
                                <template #addonAfter>元</template>
                              </a-input-number>
                            </div>

                            <!-- 日期范围 -->
                            <div
                              v-else-if="
                                [WIDGET.DATE_RANGE].includes(
                                  getWidget(condition.varName).type
                                )
                              "
                            >
                              <a-input-number
                                v-model:value="condition.val"
                                :max="99999999"
                                :formatter="(v) => ObjectUtil.limitScale(v, 1)"
                                :controls="false"
                                :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                                placeholder="请输入"
                                style="width: 100%"
                              >
                                <template #addonAfter>天</template>
                              </a-input-number>
                            </div>

                            <!-- 单选 -->
                            <div
                              v-else-if="
                                getWidget(condition.varName).type === WIDGET.SINGLE_CHOICE
                              "
                            >
                              <a-select
                                v-model:value="condition.val"
                                :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                                show-search
                                placeholder="请选择"
                                style="width: 100%"
                              >
                                <a-select-option
                                  v-for="option in getWidget(condition.varName).options"
                                  :key="option"
                                  :value="option"
                                >
                                  {{ option }}
                                </a-select-option>
                              </a-select>
                            </div>

                            <!-- 多选 -->
                            <div
                              v-else-if="
                                getWidget(condition.varName).type === WIDGET.MULTI_CHOICE
                              "
                            >
                              <a-select
                                mode="multiple"
                                v-model:value="condition.val"
                                :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                                show-search
                                placeholder="请选择"
                                :maxTagCount="isMobile ? 1 : undefined"
                                style="width: 100%"
                              >
                                <a-select-option
                                  v-for="option in getWidget(condition.varName).options"
                                  :key="option"
                                  :value="option"
                                >
                                  {{ option }}
                                </a-select-option>
                              </a-select>
                            </div>

                            <!-- 日期 -->
                            <div
                              v-else-if="
                                getWidget(condition.varName).type === WIDGET.DATE
                              "
                            >
                              <a-date-picker
                                v-model:value="condition.val"
                                :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                                style="width: 100%"
                                :getPopupContainer="
                                  isMobile ? () => document.body : undefined
                                "
                              />
                            </div>

                            <!-- 部门 -->
                            <div
                              v-else-if="
                                getWidget(condition.varName).type === WIDGET.DEPARTMENT
                              "
                            >
                              <a-select
                                mode="multiple"
                                v-model:value="condition.val"
                                :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                                show-search
                                placeholder="选择部门"
                                :maxTagCount="isMobile ? 1 : undefined"
                                style="width: 100%"
                              >
                                <a-select-option
                                  v-for="dept in allDepts"
                                  :key="dept.id"
                                  :value="dept.id"
                                >
                                  {{ dept.name }}
                                </a-select-option>
                              </a-select>
                            </div>

                            <!-- 员工 -->
                            <div
                              v-else-if="
                                getWidget(condition.varName).type === WIDGET.EMPLOYEE
                              "
                            >
                              <a-select
                                mode="multiple"
                                v-model:value="condition.val"
                                :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                                show-search
                                placeholder="选择员工"
                                :maxTagCount="isMobile ? 1 : undefined"
                                style="width: 100%"
                              >
                                <a-select-option
                                  v-for="user in allUsers"
                                  :key="user.id"
                                  :value="user.id"
                                >
                                  {{ user.name }}
                                </a-select-option>
                              </a-select>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </template>
                      </div>

                      <!-- 删除条件按钮 -->
                      <div
                        v-if="idx > 0 || conditionGroup.conditions.length > 1"
                        class="condition-actions"
                      >
                        <DeleteOutlined
                          class="condition-delete-icon"
                          @click="rmCondition(conditionGroup, condition)"
                        />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </template>
            </div>

            <div class="sub-content">
              <a-button
                type="dashed"
                @click="addCondition(conditionGroup)"
                :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                :block="isMobile"
                class="add-condition-btn"
              >
                <template #icon>
                  <PlusOutlined />
                </template>
                添加条件
              </a-button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </template>
      </div>

      <!-- 空状态 -->
      <div v-else class="empty-state">
        <div class="empty-icon">
          <FileOutlined />
        </div>
        <div class="empty-text">暂无条件</div>
        <div class="empty-hint">请添加条件组来设置分支条件</div>
      </div>

      <section class="operate">
        <a-button
          type="primary"
          @click="addConditionGroup"
          :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
          :block="isMobile"
          class="add-group-btn"
        >
          <template #icon>
            <PlusOutlined />
          </template>
          添加条件组
        </a-button>
      </section>

      <!-- 发起人选项 -->
      <OrganChooseBox
        v-model:visible="showOrganChooseBox"
        v-model:selected="selectedOrgan"
        :is-mobile="isMobile"
        title="选择发起人"
      />
    </div>

    <!-- 桌面端底部按钮 -->
    <template v-if="!isMobile" #footer>
      <a-button @click="handleCancel">取消</a-button>
      <a-button type="primary" @click="saveCondition()">保存</a-button>
    </template>
  </a-drawer>
</template>

<script setup>
import EditableText from "@/components/common/EditableText.vue";
import { WIDGET } from "@/components/flow/common/FlowConstant";
import { useOrganStore } from "@/store/organ";
import { useFlowStore } from "@/store/flow";
import {
  DeleteOutlined,
  PlusOutlined,
  LeftOutlined,
  InfoCircleOutlined,
  FileOutlined,
  RightOutlined,
} from "@ant-design/icons-vue";
import { computed, ref, toRaw, watch, onMounted, onUnmounted } from "vue";
import ArrayUtil from "../common/ArrayUtil";
import { names as FunNames, INITIATOR_VAR_NAME } from "../common/FormExp";
import ObjectUtil from "../common/ObjectUtil";
import Snowflake from "../common/Snowflake";
import OrganChooseBox from "../dialog/OrganChooseBox.vue";

const flowStore = useFlowStore();
const { getById, users: allUsers, depts: allDepts } = useOrganStore();
const { showConditionDrawer, setConditionsConfig, flowDefinition } = flowStore;
const conditionsConfig0 = computed(() => flowStore.conditionsConfig0);
const visible = ref(false);

// 检测是否为移动端
const isMobile = computed(() => {
  return window.innerWidth <= 768;
});

// 所有的条件选项
const conditionOptions = ref([]);
const _uid = ref(0);
const priorityLevel = ref(0);
const gatewayConfig = ref({});
const flowNodeConfig = ref({});
const selectedGroupCondition = ref({});

const showOrganChooseBox = ref(false);
const selectedOrgan = ref([]);

// 操作符标签映射
const operatorLabels = {
  0: "等于",
  1: "不等于",
  2: "大于",
  3: "大于等于",
  4: "小于",
  5: "小于等于",
  10: "包含",
  11: "不包含",
  12: "是",
  13: "不是",
  14: "为空",
  15: "不为空",
  20: "属于",
  21: "不属于",
};

// 获取操作符标签
const getOperatorLabel = (funIdx) => {
  return operatorLabels[funIdx] || FunNames[funIdx] || `操作${funIdx}`;
};

// 获取选项类型标签
const getOptionTypeLabel = (type) => {
  const typeMap = {
    [WIDGET.SINGLELINE_TEXT]: "文本",
    [WIDGET.NUMBER]: "数字",
    [WIDGET.MONEY]: "金额",
    [WIDGET.SINGLE_CHOICE]: "单选",
    [WIDGET.MULTI_CHOICE]: "多选",
    [WIDGET.DATE]: "日期",
    [WIDGET.DATE_RANGE]: "日期范围",
    [WIDGET.DEPARTMENT]: "部门",
    [WIDGET.EMPLOYEE]: "员工",
    [WIDGET.FORMULA]: "公式",
    [WIDGET.DETAIL]: "明细",
    initiator: "发起人",
  };
  return typeMap[type] || "";
};

// 获取用户名称
const getUserName = (userId) => {
  const user = getById(userId);
  return user?.name || `用户${userId}`;
};

// 移除用户
const removeUser = (condition, userId) => {
  if (Array.isArray(condition.val)) {
    const index = condition.val.indexOf(userId);
    if (index > -1) {
      condition.val.splice(index, 1);
    }
  }
};

const onOpenOrganChooseBox = (condition) => {
  showOrganChooseBox.value = true;
  selectedOrgan.value = condition.val || [];
  selectedGroupCondition.value = condition;
};

watch(selectedOrgan, () => {
  if (selectedGroupCondition.value) {
    selectedGroupCondition.value.val = [...selectedOrgan.value];
  }
});

// 侧边栏是否打开
watch(
  () => flowStore.isConditionDrawerOpened,
  (isOpen) => {
    visible.value = isOpen;
    if (isOpen) {
      initCondition();
      // 移动端滚动到顶部
      if (isMobile.value) {
        setTimeout(() => {
          const content = document.querySelector(".condition-drawer__content");
          if (content) content.scrollTop = 0;
        }, 100);
      }
    }
  }
);

// 侧边栏打开初始化
const initCondition = () => {
  const val = conditionsConfig0.value;
  if (!val) return;

  _uid.value = val.id;
  priorityLevel.value = val.priorityLevel;
  gatewayConfig.value = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(toRaw(val.value))); // 深拷贝
  flowNodeConfig.value =
    gatewayConfig.value.conditionNodes?.[priorityLevel.value - 1] || {};

  // 确保conditionGroups存在
  if (!flowNodeConfig.value.conditionGroups) {
    flowNodeConfig.value.conditionGroups = [];
  }

  // 初始化分组条件选项 - 修复发起人条件
  conditionOptions.value = [];

  // 添加发起人选项
  conditionOptions.value.push({
    name: INITIATOR_VAR_NAME,
    label: "发起人",
    type: "initiator",
    operators: [20, 21],
  });

  // 添加表单组件 - 修复核心问题：移除必填限制，完善所有组件类型的操作符配置
  const widgets = ObjectUtil.copy(flowDefinition.flowWidgets || []);
  if (widgets && widgets.length) {
    widgets.forEach((widget) => {
      const { name, type, label, formulaItems, details, options } = widget;

      // 克隆组件，避免影响原数据
      const widgetCopy = { ...widget };
      widgetCopy.options = options || []; // 确保options存在

      // 为所有组件配置操作符（不再限制必填）
      if ([WIDGET.SINGLELINE_TEXT].includes(type)) {
        widgetCopy.operators = [0, 1, 10, 11, 14, 15]; // 补充等于/不等于操作符
      } else if ([WIDGET.NUMBER, WIDGET.MONEY, WIDGET.DATE_RANGE].includes(type)) {
        widgetCopy.operators = [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
      } else if ([WIDGET.SINGLE_CHOICE, WIDGET.DATE].includes(type)) {
        widgetCopy.operators = [12, 13, 14, 15]; // 补充为空/不为空
      } else if ([WIDGET.MULTI_CHOICE].includes(type)) {
        widgetCopy.operators = [20, 21];
      } else if ([WIDGET.DEPARTMENT, WIDGET.EMPLOYEE].includes(type)) {
        widgetCopy.operators = [20, 21];
      } else if (type === WIDGET.FORMULA) {
        widgetCopy.operators = [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
      } else if (type === WIDGET.DETAIL) {
        widgetCopy.operators = [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
      }

      // 过滤掉没有配置操作符的组件
      if (widgetCopy.operators && widgetCopy.operators.length > 0) {
        conditionOptions.value.push(widgetCopy);
      }
    });
  }
};

// 条件选项切换
const onConditionChange = (optionName, condition) => {
  selectedGroupCondition.value = condition;
  const option = ArrayUtil.get(conditionOptions.value, "name", optionName);

  if (option) {
    // 清除选中的操作
    condition.operator = null;
    // 清除条件值
    condition.val = null;
    // 设置操作符选项
    condition.operators = option.operators || [];

    // 根据类型设置默认值 - 完善所有类型的默认值初始化
    if (
      option.type === WIDGET.MULTI_CHOICE ||
      option.type === WIDGET.DEPARTMENT ||
      option.type === WIDGET.EMPLOYEE ||
      option.name === INITIATOR_VAR_NAME
    ) {
      condition.val = [];
    } else if (option.type === WIDGET.SINGLELINE_TEXT) {
      condition.val = ""; // 文本默认空字符串
    } else if (
      [
        WIDGET.NUMBER,
        WIDGET.MONEY,
        WIDGET.DATE_RANGE,
        WIDGET.FORMULA,
        WIDGET.DETAIL,
      ].includes(option.type)
    ) {
      condition.val = 0; // 数字类型默认0
    } else if ([WIDGET.SINGLE_CHOICE, WIDGET.DATE].includes(option.type)) {
      condition.val = ""; // 单选/日期默认空字符串
    }
  }
};

// 获取组件名称
const getWidget = (name) => {
  if (name === INITIATOR_VAR_NAME) {
    return {
      name: INITIATOR_VAR_NAME,
      label: "发起人",
      type: "initiator",
      operators: [20, 21],
    };
  }
  return ArrayUtil.get(conditionOptions.value, "name", name) || {};
};

// 条件组相关操作
const addConditionGroup = () => {
  if (!flowNodeConfig.value.conditionGroups) {
    flowNodeConfig.value.conditionGroups = [];
  }
  flowNodeConfig.value.conditionGroups.push({
    id: Snowflake.generate(),
    conditions: [
      {
        id: Snowflake.generate(),
        varName: "",
        operator: null,
        val: null,
      },
    ],
  });
};

const rmConditionGroup = (conditionGroup) => {
  ArrayUtil.remove(flowNodeConfig.value.conditionGroups, "id", conditionGroup.id);
};

const addCondition = (conditionGroup) => {
  conditionGroup.conditions.push({
    id: Snowflake.generate(),
    varName: "",
    operator: null,
    val: null,
  });
};

const rmCondition = (conditionGroup, condition) => {
  ArrayUtil.remove(conditionGroup.conditions, "id", condition.id);
};

// 编辑节点名称
const onNodeNameChange = (name) => {
  flowNodeConfig.value.name = name;
  saveCondition(false);
};

// 移动端取消处理
const handleCancel = () => {
  onClose();
};

const saveCondition = (leave = true) => {
  if (!gatewayConfig.value || !flowNodeConfig.value) return;

  // 深拷贝当前配置，避免引用问题
  const nodeConfig = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(toRaw(flowNodeConfig.value)));

  // 过滤空条件
  if (nodeConfig.conditionGroups) {
    nodeConfig.conditionGroups = nodeConfig.conditionGroups.filter((group) => {
      if (group.conditions) {
        group.conditions = group.conditions.filter((condition) => {
          // 更严格的条件验证
          if (!condition.varName) return false;
          if (condition.operator === null || condition.operator === undefined)
            return false;

          // 验证条件值 - 完善不同类型的值验证逻辑
          if (condition.varName === INITIATOR_VAR_NAME) {
            return (
              condition.val && Array.isArray(condition.val) && condition.val.length > 0
            );
          } else {
            const widget = getWidget(condition.varName);
            if (
              widget.type === WIDGET.MULTI_CHOICE ||
              widget.type === WIDGET.DEPARTMENT ||
              widget.type === WIDGET.EMPLOYEE
            ) {
              return (
                condition.val && Array.isArray(condition.val) && condition.val.length > 0
              );
            }
            // 文本类型允许空字符串（配合为空/不为空操作符）
            else if (widget.type === WIDGET.SINGLELINE_TEXT) {
              return condition.val !== null && condition.val !== undefined;
            }
            // 数字类型允许0值
            else if (
              [
                WIDGET.NUMBER,
                WIDGET.MONEY,
                WIDGET.DATE_RANGE,
                WIDGET.FORMULA,
                WIDGET.DETAIL,
              ].includes(widget.type)
            ) {
              return condition.val !== null && condition.val !== undefined;
            }
            // 单选/日期类型
            else {
              return (
                condition.val !== null &&
                condition.val !== undefined &&
                condition.val !== ""
              );
            }
          }
        });
      }
      return group.conditions && group.conditions.length > 0;
    });
  }

  // 确保网关配置存在
  if (!gatewayConfig.value.conditionNodes) {
    gatewayConfig.value.conditionNodes = [];
  }

  // 更新分支节点配置
  gatewayConfig.value.conditionNodes[priorityLevel.value - 1] = nodeConfig;

  // 确保网关节点有默认分支
  if (gatewayConfig.value.conditionNodes.length > 0) {
    const lastNode =
      gatewayConfig.value.conditionNodes[gatewayConfig.value.conditionNodes.length - 1];
    if (!lastNode.conditionGroups || lastNode.conditionGroups.length === 0) {
      // 最后一个是默认分支，不需要条件
    }
  }

  // 保存到Store
  setConditionsConfig({
    value: toRaw(gatewayConfig.value),
    priorityLevel: priorityLevel.value,
    flag: true,
    id: _uid.value,
  });

  if (leave) {
    showConditionDrawer(false);
  }
};

const onClose = () => {
  saveCondition();
};

// 移动端手势支持
const handleTouchMove = (event) => {
  event.stopPropagation();
};

onMounted(() => {
  if (isMobile.value) {
    document.addEventListener("touchmove", handleTouchMove, { passive: false });
  }
});

onUnmounted(() => {
  if (isMobile.value) {
    document.removeEventListener("touchmove", handleTouchMove);
  }
});
</script>

// 移动端特定样式
@media (max-width: 768px) {
  .condition-drawer__content {
    .condition-group-editor {
      .condition-item {
        position: relative;

        .condition-row {
          .condition-relation {
            position: absolute;
            left: 0;
            top: 0;
          }

          .condition-content-wrapper {
            padding-left: 30px;
          }
        }
      }
    }

    // 移动端选择器下拉框样式
    .mobile-select-dropdown {
      .ant-select-item {
        padding: 12px;
        font-size: 14px;

        .option-content {
          .option-type {
            font-size: 11px;
          }
        }
      }
    }

    // 移动端日期选择器
    .ant-picker-panel {
      .ant-picker-cell {
        height: 44px;
        line-height: 44px;
      }
    }
  }
}

// 优化移动端滚动
@media (max-width: 768px) {
  .ant-drawer-content-wrapper {
    overscroll-behavior: contain;
  }

  .condition-drawer__content {
    * {
      -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent;
    }
  }
}
</style>

flow/drawer/copyerDrawer.vue

<template>
  <!-- 移动端全屏抽屉 -->
  <a-drawer
    v-if="visible"
    :visible="visible"
    :width="isMobile ? '100%' : 540"
    :placement="isMobile ? 'bottom' : 'right'"
    :height="isMobile ? '85vh' : undefined"
    :closable="!isMobile"
    :mask-closable="isMobile"
    :body-style="{ padding: 0 }"
    :footer="!isMobile"
    :class="['copyer-drawer', { 'mobile-drawer': isMobile }]"
    @close="handleCancel"
  >
    <!-- 移动端标题栏 -->
    <template #title v-if="isMobile">
      <div class="mobile-drawer-header">
        <div class="mobile-header-left">
          <a-button
            type="text"
            size="small"
            @click="handleCancel"
            class="mobile-close-btn"
          >
            <LeftOutlined />
          </a-button>
          <EditableText
            :value="flowNodeConfig.name"
            @change="onNodeNameChange"
            class="mobile-title"
            :compact="isMobile"
          />
        </div>
        <a-button type="primary" size="small" @click="saveCc()" class="mobile-save-btn">
          保存
        </a-button>
      </div>
    </template>

    <!-- 桌面端标题 -->
    <template #title v-else>
      <EditableText :value="flowNodeConfig.name" @change="onNodeNameChange" />
    </template>

    <div class="copyer-drawer__content" :class="{ 'mobile-content': isMobile }">
      <div class="copyer-editor-tab-wrapper">
        <!-- 移动端标签切换 -->
        <div class="mobile-tab-header" v-if="isMobile">
          <div class="mobile-tab-item active">
            <SendOutlined />
            <span>设置抄送人</span>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- 桌面端标签切换 -->
        <a-radio-group
          v-model:value="viewEditorType"
          button-style="solid"
          class="desktop-tab-group"
          v-else
        >
          <a-radio-button :value="0">设置抄送人</a-radio-button>
          <!-- <a-radio-button :value="1">表单权限</a-radio-button> -->
        </a-radio-group>

        <!-- 抄送人设置 -->
        <div class="item-content-editor" v-if="viewEditorType == 0">
          <div class="content-wrap">
            <div class="item-content">
              <!-- 抄送人列表 -->
              <div class="item-wrap approver">
                <div
                  class="approver-list"
                  v-if="flowNodeConfig.ccs && flowNodeConfig.ccs.length > 0"
                >
                  <div
                    class="approver-wrapper"
                    v-for="(item, idx) in flowNodeConfig.ccs"
                    :key="item.rid"
                  >
                    <div class="header">
                      <span class="header-title">抄送人{{ idx + 1 }}</span>
                      <DeleteOutlined
                        class="delete-icon"
                        :style="{ fontSize: isMobile ? '16px' : '18px' }"
                        @click="rmCC(item)"
                        v-if="flowNodeConfig.ccs.length > 1"
                      />
                    </div>
                    <div class="main-content">
                      <a-radio-group
                        class="radio-group"
                        v-model:value="item.ccType"
                        @change="onCcTypeChanged(item)"
                        :size="isMobile ? 'small' : 'middle'"
                      >
                        <a-row :gutter="[8, 8]">
                          <a-col
                            v-for="option in ccOptions"
                            :key="option.value"
                            :span="isMobile ? 12 : 8"
                          >
                            <a-radio :value="option.value" class="cc-radio">
                              <span class="radio-label">{{ option.label }}</span>
                            </a-radio>
                          </a-col>
                        </a-row>
                      </a-radio-group>
                    </div>
                    <div class="sub-content" v-if="![0, 6].includes(item.ccType)">
                      <div class="sub-content-top-line"></div>

                      <!-- 上级选择 -->
                      <template v-if="item.ccType == 1">
                        <p class="bold">请选择上级</p>
                        <div class="form-item-wrapper">
                          <div class="form-label">发起人的</div>
                          <a-select
                            v-model:value="item.layer"
                            placeholder="请选择上级"
                            :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                            :popup-class-name="isMobile ? 'mobile-select-dropdown' : ''"
                          >
                            <template #dropdownRender>
                              <div>
                                <div class="switch-container">
                                  <div class="select-tip">从直属上级向上选择</div>
                                  <a-button
                                    type="link"
                                    @click="switchLayerType(item)"
                                    class="switch-link"
                                  >
                                    <SwapOutlined />
                                    {{
                                      item.layerType == 0
                                        ? "切为最高上级向下"
                                        : "切为直属上级向上"
                                    }}
                                  </a-button>
                                </div>
                                <a-divider style="margin: 8px 0" />
                              </div>
                            </template>
                            <a-select-option v-for="i in 20" :value="i - 1" :key="i">
                              <template v-if="item.layerType == 0">
                                {{
                                  i == 1 ? "直属上级" : "直属上级加 " + (i - 1) + " 级"
                                }}
                              </template>
                              <template v-else>
                                {{
                                  i == 1 ? "最高上级" : "最高上级减 " + (i - 1) + " 级"
                                }}
                              </template>
                            </a-select-option>
                          </a-select>
                        </div>
                      </template>

                      <!-- 部门负责人选择 -->
                      <template v-else-if="item.ccType == 2">
                        <p class="bold">请选择部门负责人</p>
                        <div class="form-item-wrapper">
                          <div class="form-label">发起人的</div>
                          <a-select
                            v-model:value="item.layer"
                            placeholder="请选择部门负责人"
                            :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                          >
                            <template #dropdownRender>
                              <div>
                                <div class="switch-container">
                                  <div class="select-tip">从直属部门负责人向上选择</div>
                                  <a-button
                                    type="link"
                                    @click="switchLayerType(item)"
                                    class="switch-link"
                                  >
                                    <SwapOutlined />
                                    {{
                                      item.layerType == 0
                                        ? "切为最高部门向下"
                                        : "切为直属部门向上"
                                    }}
                                  </a-button>
                                </div>
                                <a-divider style="margin: 8px 0" />
                              </div>
                            </template>
                            <a-select-option v-for="i in 20" :value="i - 1" :key="i">
                              <template v-if="item.layerType == 0">
                                {{
                                  i == 1
                                    ? "直属部门负责人"
                                    : "直属部门负责人加 " + (i - 1) + " 级"
                                }}
                              </template>
                              <template v-else>
                                {{
                                  i == 1
                                    ? "最高部门负责人"
                                    : "最高部门负责人减 " + (i - 1) + " 级"
                                }}
                              </template>
                            </a-select-option>
                          </a-select>
                        </div>
                      </template>

                      <!-- 角色选择 -->
                      <template v-else-if="item.ccType == 3">
                        <p class="bold">选择角色</p>
                        <div class="form-item-wrapper">
                          <div class="form-label">组织角色</div>
                          <a-select
                            v-model:value="item.roles"
                            mode="multiple"
                            placeholder="请选择角色"
                            :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                            :max-tag-count="isMobile ? 1 : undefined"
                          >
                            <a-select-option
                              v-for="role in allRoles"
                              :value="role.id"
                              :key="role.id"
                            >
                              {{ role.name }}
                            </a-select-option>
                          </a-select>
                        </div>
                      </template>

                      <!-- 指定成员选择 -->
                      <template v-else-if="item.ccType == 4">
                        <p class="bold">
                          添加成员
                          <span class="hint-text">（不能超过 25 人）</span>
                        </p>
                        <div class="assignee-box">
                          <a-button
                            size="small"
                            @click="onAssigneeClick(item)"
                            :shape="isMobile ? 'circle' : 'default'"
                            class="add-member-btn"
                          >
                            <PlusOutlined />
                          </a-button>
                          <div class="assignee-list">
                            <a-tag
                              v-for="userId in item.assignees"
                              :key="userId"
                              :size="isMobile ? 'small' : 'middle'"
                              closable
                              @close="removeAssignee(item, userId)"
                              class="member-tag"
                            >
                              {{ getUserById(userId).name }}
                            </a-tag>
                            <div
                              v-if="!item.assignees || item.assignees.length === 0"
                              class="empty-hint"
                            >
                              点击上方按钮添加成员
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </template>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>

                <!-- 空状态 -->
                <div class="empty-state" v-else>
                  <div class="empty-icon">
                    <TeamOutlined />
                  </div>
                  <div class="empty-text">暂未设置抄送人</div>
                  <div class="empty-hint">抄送人将收到流程通知但无需审批</div>
                </div>

                <!-- 添加抄送人按钮 -->
                <div class="add-operator">
                  <a-button
                    type="dashed"
                    @click="addCC"
                    :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                    :block="isMobile"
                    class="add-cc-btn"
                  >
                    <template #icon>
                      <PlusOutlined />
                    </template>
                    {{
                      flowNodeConfig.ccs && flowNodeConfig.ccs.length > 0
                        ? "继续添加抄送人"
                        : "添加抄送人"
                    }}
                  </a-button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- 设置表单权限 -->
        <NodeFormAuthSetting
          v-model:flowNodeConfig="flowNodeConfig"
          :editable="false"
          :is-mobile="isMobile"
          v-else-if="viewEditorType == 1"
        ></NodeFormAuthSetting>
      </div>

      <!-- 成员选择对话框 -->
      <OrganChooseBox
        v-if="showChooseOrgan"
        v-model:visible="showChooseOrgan"
        v-model:selected="selectedAssignee.assignees"
        :hidden-dept="true"
        :hidden-role="true"
        :is-mobile="isMobile"
        title="选择抄送人"
      />
    </div>

    <!-- 桌面端底部按钮 -->
    <template #footer v-if="!isMobile">
      <div style="display: flex; justify-content: flex-end; gap: 8px">
        <a-button @click="handleCancel">取消</a-button>
        <a-button type="primary" @click="saveCc()">保存</a-button>
      </div>
    </template>
  </a-drawer>
</template>

<script setup>
import EditableText from "@/components/common/EditableText.vue";
import { useFlowStore } from "@/store/flow";
import { useOrganStore } from "@/store/organ";
import {
  DeleteOutlined,
  PlusOutlined,
  SwapOutlined,
  LeftOutlined,
  SendOutlined,
  TeamOutlined,
} from "@ant-design/icons-vue";
import { computed, onMounted, ref, toRaw, watch, onUnmounted } from "vue";
import ArrayUtil from "../common/ArrayUtil";
import Snowflake from "../common/Snowflake";
import OrganChooseBox from "../dialog/OrganChooseBox.vue";
import NodeFormAuthSetting from "../NodeFormAuthSetting.vue";

let flowStore = useFlowStore();
let { allRoles, getUserById } = useOrganStore();
let { showCopyerDrawer, setCopyerConfig } = flowStore;
let isCopyerDrawerOpened = computed(() => flowStore.isCopyerDrawerOpened);
let copyerConfig0 = computed(() => flowStore.copyerConfig0);

// 检测是否为移动端
const isMobile = computed(() => {
  return window.innerWidth <= 768;
});

let visible = computed({
  get: () => isCopyerDrawerOpened.value,
  set: () => closeDrawer(),
});

let _uid = ref(0);
let flowNodeConfig = ref({});
const viewEditorType = ref(0);

// 抄送人选项配置
const ccOptions = computed(() => [
  { label: "发起人本人", value: 0 },
  { label: "上级", value: 1 },
  { label: "部门负责人", value: 2 },
  { label: "指定成员", value: 4 },
  // { label: '发起人自选', value: 6 },
]);

// 切换上级和部门负责人的人事层级关系
const switchLayerType = (cc) => {
  cc.layerType = cc.layerType == 0 ? 1 : 0;
};

// 抄送人选择指定成员
let showChooseOrgan = ref(false);
let selectedAssignee = ref({});

const onAssigneeClick = (item) => {
  selectedAssignee.value = item;
  showChooseOrgan.value = true;
};

// 移除指定成员
const removeAssignee = (item, userId) => {
  if (item.assignees) {
    const index = item.assignees.indexOf(userId);
    if (index > -1) {
      item.assignees.splice(index, 1);
    }
  }
};

// 抄送人类型变更事件
const onCcTypeChanged = (cc) => {
  const { ccType } = cc;

  // 重置相关字段
  const fieldsToDelete = ["layerType", "layer", "roles", "assignees"];

  fieldsToDelete.forEach((field) => {
    if (field in cc) {
      delete cc[field];
    }
  });

  // 根据类型设置默认值
  if ([1, 2].includes(ccType)) {
    cc.layer = 0;
    cc.layerType = 0;
  } else if (ccType === 4) {
    cc.assignees = [];
  }
};

// 添加抄送人
const addCC = () => {
  if (!flowNodeConfig.value.ccs) {
    flowNodeConfig.value.ccs = [];
  }
  flowNodeConfig.value.ccs.push({
    rid: Snowflake.generate(),
    ccType: 0,
  });
};

// 删除抄送人
const rmCC = (cc) => {
  ArrayUtil.remove(flowNodeConfig.value.ccs, "rid", cc.rid);
};

watch(
  copyerConfig0,
  (val) => {
    if (val?.value) {
      flowNodeConfig.value = { ...val.value };
      viewEditorType.value = 0;
      _uid.value = val.id;

      // 确保ccs数组存在
      if (!flowNodeConfig.value.ccs) {
        flowNodeConfig.value.ccs = [];
      }
    }
  },
  { immediate: true }
);

// 编辑节点名称
const onNodeNameChange = (name) => {
  flowNodeConfig.value.name = name;
  saveCc(false);
};

// 移动端取消处理
const handleCancel = () => {
  if (isMobile.value) {
    // 可以添加未保存提示
    closeDrawer();
  } else {
    closeDrawer();
  }
};

const saveCc = (leave = true) => {
  setCopyerConfig({
    value: toRaw(flowNodeConfig.value),
    flag: true,
    id: _uid.value,
  });
  leave && closeDrawer();
};

const closeDrawer = () => {
  showCopyerDrawer(false);
};

// 移动端手势支持
const handleTouchMove = (event) => {
  event.stopPropagation();
};

onMounted(() => {
  if (isMobile.value) {
    document.addEventListener("touchmove", handleTouchMove, { passive: false });
  }
});

onUnmounted(() => {
  if (isMobile.value) {
    document.removeEventListener("touchmove", handleTouchMove);
  }
});
</script>

    }

// 优化移动端滚动
@media (max-width: 768px) {
  .ant-drawer-content {
    overscroll-behavior: contain;
  }

  .copyer-drawer__content {
    * {
      -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent;
    }
  }
}
</style>

flow/drwaer/PromoterDrawer.vue

<template>
  <!-- 移动端全屏抽屉 -->
  <a-drawer
    :width="isMobile ? '100%' : 540"
    :title="isMobile ? undefined : '发起人设置'"
    :visible="visible"
    :closable="!isMobile"
    :mask-closable="isMobile"
    :placement="isMobile ? 'bottom' : 'right'"
    :height="isMobile ? '75vh' : undefined"
    :class="['promoter-drawer', { 'mobile-drawer': isMobile }]"
    :destroy-on-close="true"
    @close="handleCancel"
  >
    <!-- 移动端自定义标题 -->
    <template v-if="isMobile" #title>
      <div class="mobile-drawer-header">
        <div class="mobile-header-left">
          <a-button
            type="text"
            size="small"
            @click="handleCancel"
            class="mobile-close-btn"
          >
            <LeftOutlined />
          </a-button>
          <div class="mobile-title">发起人设置</div>
        </div>
        <div class="mobile-header-right">
          <a-button type="primary" size="small" @click="savePromoter">保存</a-button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </template>

    <div class="promoter-drawer__content" :class="{ 'mobile-content': isMobile }">
      <!-- 发起人设置 -->
      <div class="approval-editor-content">
        <div class="item-content-editor">
          <div class="content-wrap">
            <!-- 设置说明（移动端） -->
            <div class="setting-intro" v-if="isMobile">
              <InfoCircleOutlined />
              <span>设置谁可以发起此流程</span>
            </div>

            <div class="item-content">
              <!-- 类型提示 -->
              <div class="type-prompt">谁可以发起该审批</div>

              <!-- 类型选择 -->
              <div class="type-select-wrapper">
                <a-select
                  class="type-content"
                  v-model:value="flowPermission.type"
                  @change="handleInitiatorTypeChange"
                  placeholder="请选择"
                  :size="isMobile ? 'large' : 'middle'"
                >
                  <a-select-option :value="0">全员</a-select-option>
                  <a-select-option :value="1">指定人员</a-select-option>
                  <a-select-option :value="2">均不可提交</a-select-option>
                </a-select>

                <!-- 类型说明 -->
                <div class="type-description">
                  <div v-if="flowPermission.type === 0" class="desc-item">
                    <CheckCircleOutlined class="success-icon" />
                    <span>所有成员均可发起此流程</span>
                  </div>
                  <div v-else-if="flowPermission.type === 1" class="desc-item">
                    <UserOutlined class="info-icon" />
                    <span>仅指定人员可以发起</span>
                  </div>
                  <div v-else-if="flowPermission.type === 2" class="desc-item">
                    <InfoCircleOutlined />
                    <span>暂时关闭此流程的发起</span>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>

              <!-- 指定人员选择 -->
              <template v-if="flowPermission.type == 1">
                <div class="selected-content">
                  <!-- 已选人员列表 -->
                  <div class="selected-header">
                    <div class="selected-count">
                      <UserOutlined />
                      <span>已选择 {{ selected.length }} 人</span>
                    </div>
                    <a-button
                      type="primary"
                      ghost
                      size="small"
                      @click="openInitiatorChooseBox"
                      class="add-more-btn"
                    >
                      <template #icon>
                        <PlusOutlined />
                      </template>
                      添加人员
                    </a-button>
                  </div>

                  <!-- 人员列表 -->
                  <div class="selected-list" v-if="selected.length > 0">
                    <div class="user-list">
                      <div class="user-item" v-for="item in selected" :key="item.id">
                        <div class="user-avatar">
                          {{ getAvatarText(getUserInfo(item.id)?.name) }}
                        </div>
                        <div class="user-info">
                          <div class="user-name">
                            {{ getUserInfo(item.id)?.name || "未知用户" }}
                          </div>
                          <div class="user-dept" v-if="getUserInfo(item.id)?.department">
                            {{ getUserInfo(item.id)?.department }}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                        <DeleteOutlined
                          class="delete-user"
                          @click="removeUser(item.id)"
                        />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  <!-- 空状态 -->
                  <div class="empty-state" v-else>
                    <UserAddOutlined class="empty-icon" />
                    <div class="empty-text">暂无选择人员</div>
                    <div class="empty-hint">点击"添加人员"按钮选择发起人</div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </template>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- PC端底部按钮 -->
    <template #footer v-if="!isMobile">
      <div class="drawer-footer">
        <a-button @click="handleCancel">取消</a-button>
        <a-button type="primary" @click="savePromoter">保存</a-button>
      </div>
    </template>

    <!-- 人员选择对话框 -->
    <OrganChooseBox
      v-if="initiatorChooseBoxVisible"
      :visible="initiatorChooseBoxVisible"
      :selected="selected"
      :only-id="false"
      :is-mobile="isMobile"
      title="选择发起人"
      @update:visible="(val) => (initiatorChooseBoxVisible = val)"
      @update:selected="(val) => (selected = val)"
    />
  </a-drawer>
</template>

<script setup>
import { useFlowStore } from "@/store/flow";
import { useOrganStore } from "@/store/organ";
import { computed, ref, watch, toRaw, onMounted, onUnmounted } from "vue";
import OrganChooseBox from "../dialog/OrganChooseBox.vue";
import {
  LeftOutlined,
  UserOutlined,
  TeamOutlined,
  PlusOutlined,
  DeleteOutlined,
  CheckCircleOutlined,
  InfoCircleOutlined,
  UserAddOutlined,
} from "@ant-design/icons-vue";

// Stores
const flowStore = useFlowStore();
const organStore = useOrganStore();
const { getById } = organStore;
const { showPromoterDrawer, setPromoterConfig } = flowStore;

// Computed
const isPromoterDrawerOpened = computed(() => flowStore.isPromoterDrawerOpened);
const promoterConfig0 = computed(() => flowStore.promoterConfig0);

// State
const initiatorChooseBoxVisible = ref(false);
const selected = ref([]);
const _uid = ref(0);
const isMobile = ref(false);

const flowPermission = ref({
  type: 0,
  flowInitiators: [],
});

// 检测移动端
const checkMobile = () => {
  isMobile.value = window.innerWidth <= 768;
};

onMounted(() => {
  checkMobile();
  window.addEventListener("resize", checkMobile);
});

onUnmounted(() => {
  window.removeEventListener("resize", checkMobile);
});

// Drawer visible
const visible = computed({
  get: () => isPromoterDrawerOpened.value,
  set: (val) => {
    if (!val) closeDrawer();
  },
});

// 用户信息缓存
const userInfoCache = new Map();
const getUserInfo = (userId) => {
  if (!userId) return null;
  if (userInfoCache.has(userId)) {
    return userInfoCache.get(userId);
  }
  const info = getById(userId);
  if (info) {
    userInfoCache.set(userId, info);
  }
  return info;
};

// 获取头像文本
const getAvatarText = (name) => {
  if (!name) return "?";
  return name.charAt(0).toUpperCase();
};

// 移除用户
const removeUser = (userId) => {
  selected.value = selected.value.filter((item) => item.id !== userId);
};

// 清空所有
const clearAll = () => {
  selected.value = [];
};

// 打开选择框
const openInitiatorChooseBox = () => {
  initiatorChooseBoxVisible.value = true;
};

// 类型变更
const handleInitiatorTypeChange = (type) => {
  if (type !== 1) {
    selected.value = [];
  }
};

// 监听配置变化
watch(
  promoterConfig0,
  (newVal) => {
    if (newVal?.value && visible.value) {
      try {
        flowPermission.value = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(newVal.value));

        if (Array.isArray(flowPermission.value.flowInitiators)) {
          selected.value = flowPermission.value.flowInitiators.map((item) => {
            const id = typeof item === "object" ? item.id : item;
            return { id: String(id) };
          });
        }

        _uid.value = newVal.id;
      } catch (e) {
        console.error("解析配置失败:", e);
      }
    }
  },
  { deep: true }
);

// 打开时加载数据
watch(visible, (newVal) => {
  if (newVal && promoterConfig0.value?.value) {
    try {
      const config = promoterConfig0.value.value;
      flowPermission.value = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(config));

      if (Array.isArray(config.flowInitiators)) {
        selected.value = config.flowInitiators.map((item) => {
          const id = typeof item === "object" ? item.id : item;
          return { id: String(id) };
        });
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error("加载配置失败:", e);
    }
  }
});

// 取消
const handleCancel = () => {
  closeDrawer();
};

// 保存
const savePromoter = () => {
  // 准备保存数据
  flowPermission.value.flowInitiators = selected.value.map((item) => item.id);

  setPromoterConfig({
    value: toRaw(flowPermission.value),
    flag: true,
    id: _uid.value,
  });

  closeDrawer();
};

// 关闭抽屉
const closeDrawer = () => {
  showPromoterDrawer(false);
  // 清空缓存
  userInfoCache.clear();
  // 清空选择
  selected.value = [];
  // 重置类型
  flowPermission.value = {
    type: 0,
    flowInitiators: [],
  };
};
</script>
