                  前加签
                  <a-tooltip
                    content="在当前节点之前增加一个审批节点，当新增的节点同意后，再流转至当前节点。"
                    mini
                  >
                    <icon-question-circle class="modify-sign-tip" />
                  </a-tooltip>
                </a-radio>
                <a-radio :value="CMD.ADD_SIGN">
                  并加签
                  <a-tooltip content="在当前节点同步增加其他审批人。" mini>
                    <icon-question-circle class="modify-sign-tip" />
                  </a-tooltip>
                </a-radio>
                <a-radio :value="CMD.ADD_AFTER_SIGN">
                  后加签
                  <a-tooltip
                    content="在当前节点之后增加一个审批节点，当前节点会默认同意，并流转至新增的节点。"
                    mini
                  >
                    <icon-question-circle class="modify-sign-tip" />
                  </a-tooltip>
                </a-radio>
              </a-radio-group>
            </a-form-item>

            <a-form-item
              field="userId"
              label="给谁加签"
              :required="
                [CMD.ADD_BEFORE_SIGN, CMD.ADD_AFTER_SIGN, CMD.ADD_SIGN].includes(
                  handleModalForm.flowCmd
                )
              "
            >
              <a-select
                v-model:model-value="handleModalForm.userId"
                allow-search
                placeholder="请选择加签人员"
              >
                <a-option
                  v-for="user in users"
                  :value="user.id"
                  :label="user.name"
                  :key="user"
                />
              </a-select>
            </a-form-item>
          </template>

          <a-form-item
            field="userId"
            label="给谁减签"
            :required="handleModalForm.flowCmd == CMD.DEL_SIGN"
            v-if="handleModalForm.flowCmd == CMD.DEL_SIGN"
          >
            <a-select
              v-model:model-value="handleModalForm.userId"
              allow-search
              placeholder="请选择减签人员"
            >
              <a-option
                v-for="user in users.filter((i) => deleteableUserIds.includes(i.id))"
                :key="user"
                :value="user.id"
                :label="user.name"
              />
            </a-select>
          </a-form-item>

          <template v-if="handleModalForm.flowCmd == CMD.BACK">
            <!-- <div class="action-tip">将流程回退到之前某一节点重新审批。例如发现之前审批有误时，可以将流程回退到该节点。</div> -->
            <a-form-item
              field="flowNodeId"
              label="回退到"
              :required="handleModalForm.flowCmd == CMD.BACK"
            >
              <a-select
                v-model:model-value="handleModalForm.flowNodeId"
                allow-search
                placeholder="请选择回退节点"
              >
                <a-option
                  v-for="node in jumpableNodes"
                  :key="node"
                  :value="node.id"
                  :label="node.name"
                />
              </a-select>
            </a-form-item>
          </template>

          <a-form-item
            field="comment"
            :label="handleModalCommentLabel(handleModalForm.flowCmd)"
            :required="handleModalForm.flowCmd == CMD.COMMENT"
          >
            <a-textarea
              v-model:model-value="handleModalForm.comment"
              :placeholder="`请输入${handleModalCommentLabel(handleModalForm.flowCmd)}`"
              allow-clear
              :max-length="128"
              show-word-limit
            />
          </a-form-item>

          <a-form-item field="fileIds" label="附件">
            <a-upload
              v-model:file-list="handleModalForm.fileIds"
              :action="FILE_UPLOAD_URL"
              :headers="fileUploadHeaders"
              :with-credentials="true"
              multiple
              :limit="3"
              class="action-attachment"
              @change="handleFileListChange"
            >
              <template #upload-button>
                <a-button>
                  <template #icon><icon-attachment /></template>上传
                </a-button>
              </template>
            </a-upload>
          </a-form-item>

          <!-- 签名 -->
          <template v-if="handleModalForm.flowCmd == CMD.APPROVED && flowInst.signature">
            <a-form-item field="signature" label="签名" :required="flowInst.signature">
              <div class="action-signature-box">
                <SignaturePad
                  width="480px"
                  height="200px"
                  @ok="handleSignatureOk"
                  @clear="handleSignatureCancel"
                />
              </div>
            </a-form-item>
          </template>
        </a-form>
      </div>
    </a-modal>

    <a-drawer
      :width="500"
      :visible="launchVisible"
      :mask-closable="false"
      :closable="false"
      unmountOnClose
      :header="false"
      :footer="false"
      @cancel="onLaunchClose()"
    >
      <template #title> {{ relaunchFlow.name }} </template>
      <flow-launch
        v-if="launchVisible"
        :flow="relaunchFlow"
        :relaunchFlowForm="relaunchFlowForm"
        :flowWidgets="formWidgets"
        @onCancel="onLaunchClose()"
        @onSuccess="onLaunchClose()"
      ></flow-launch>
    </a-drawer>
  </section>
</template>

<script setup>
import { FILE_DOWNLOAD_URL, FILE_PREVIEW_URL, FILE_UPLOAD_URL } from "@/api/FileApi";
import FlowInstApi from "@/api/FlowInstApi";
import FlowManApi from "@/api/FlowManApi";
import OrganApi from "@/api/OrganApi";
import FlowNodeAvatar from "@/components/common/FlowNodeAvatar.vue";
import FlowNodeRoleAvatar from "@/components/common/FlowNodeRoleAvatar.vue";
import SignaturePad from "@/components/common/SignaturePad.vue";
import ArrayUtil from "@/components/flow/common/ArrayUtil";
import {
  CMD,
  NODE,
  NODE_SIGN,
  STATUS,
  STATUS_LIST,
  WIDGET,
} from "@/components/flow/common/FlowConstant";
import ObjectUtil from "@/components/flow/common/ObjectUtil";
import { useOrganStore } from "@/stores";
import { getToken } from "@/utils/auth";
import { Message } from "@arco-design/web-vue";
import {
  IconAttachment,
  IconBackward,
  IconCheck,
  IconClose,
  IconDown,
  IconDownload,
  IconDriveFile,
  IconEdit,
  IconHistory,
  IconMessage,
  IconPenFill,
  IconPrinter,
  IconQuestionCircle,
  IconRedo,
  IconRobot,
  IconStamp,
  IconSwap,
  IconUndo,
  IconUserAdd,
} from "@arco-design/web-vue/es/icon";
import { computed, onMounted, ref, watch } from "vue";
import FormDetail from "./flow-form-detail.vue";
import FlowLaunch from "./flow-launch.vue";
import FlowPrint from "./flow-print.vue";
import FlowStatusStamp from "./flow-status-stamp.vue";
import FormEditRecord from "./form-edit-record.vue";
import FormEdit from "./form-edit.vue";

let organStore = useOrganStore();
let users = computed(() => organStore.users);

let props = defineProps({
  flowInst: { type: Object, default: () => {} },
  cancelable: { type: Boolean, default: false }, // 撤销按钮
  commentable: { type: Boolean, default: true }, // 评论按钮
  actionable: { type: Boolean, default: false }, // 其他操作按钮
  editable: { type: Boolean, default: false }, // 表单是否可以编辑
  relaunchable: { type: Boolean, default: false }, // 再次申请按钮
});
let emits = defineEmits(["onRemove", "update:flowInst"]);

let fileUploadHeaders = ref({ Authorization: getToken() }); // 文件上传请求头

let formWidgets = ref([]);
let formWidgetMap = ref({});
let flowNodes = ref([]); // 已经执行和正在执行节点
let flowFutureNodes = ref([]); // 未执行的节点
let formValue = ref({});
let formattedFormValue = ref({});
let finished = computed(() => props.flowInst.status != 0);
let loading = ref(false);

// 查询表单组件
const loadFormWidgets = () => {
  return FlowInstApi.getForm({
    flowInstId: props.flowInst.id,
    flowNodeId: props.flowInst.nodeId,
  }).then((resp) => {
    if (resp.code == 1) {
      let form = resp.data || {};
      let widgets = form.formWidgets;
      let values = form.formValue;
      let formattedValue = form.formattedFormValue;
      formWidgets.value = widgets;
      formWidgetMap.value = FlowManApi.formWidgetListToMap(widgets);
      formValue.value = JSON.parse(values);
      formattedFormValue.value = JSON.parse(formattedValue);
    }
  });
};

// 获取审批节点
const loadFlowDetail = () => {
  FlowInstApi.getDetail({ flowInstId: props.flowInst.id }).then((resp) => {
    if (resp.code == 1) {
      let { nodes, futureNodes } = resp.data;
      flowNodes.value = nodes || [];
      flowFutureNodes.value = futureNodes || [];
    }
  });
};

// 附件下载
const onAttachmentDownload = (attachment, evt) => {
  evt.stopPropagation();
  window.open(`${FILE_DOWNLOAD_URL}?id=${attachment.id}`, "_blank");
};

// 上传组件列表变化
const handleFileListChange = (fileList, fileItem) => {
  let { response: resp } = fileItem;
  if (!!!resp) return;
  if (resp.code == 1) {
    // 上传成功转换数据
    let data = resp.data;
    data.url = `${FILE_DOWNLOAD_URL}?id=${data.id}`;
    for (let i = 0; i < fileList.length; i++) {
      if (fileList[i].uid == fileItem.uid) {
        fileList[i] = data;
        return;
      }
    }
  } else {
    // 上传失败提示，删除文件
    Message.error(`文件上传失败，原因是：${resp.msg}！`);
    ArrayUtil.remove(fileList, "uid", fileItem.uid);
  }
};

// 打印相关
let showPrintModal = ref(false);
const onPrintClicked = () => {
  showPrintModal.value = true;
};

// 处理流程弹窗相关
let jumpableNodes = ref([]);
let deleteableUserIds = ref([]);
let showHandleModal = ref(false);
let handleModalTitle = ref("");
let handleModalForm = ref({});

const onHandleModalCancel = () => {
  showHandleModal.value = false;
  handleModalTitle.value = "";
  handleModalForm.value = {
    flowInstId: null, // 流程实例id
    taskId: null, // 任务id
    flowCmd: null, // 任务指令
    assignee: null, // 指派人
    comment: null, // 备注
  };
};

// 审批签字
const handleSignatureOk = (signature) => {
  handleModalForm.value.base64SignatureData = signature;
};
const handleSignatureCancel = () => {
  handleModalForm.value.base64SignatureData = null;
};

// 流程处理弹窗是否被提交
const handleFormSubmitable = computed(() => {
  let needSignature = props.flowInst.signature;
  if (handleModalForm.value.flowCmd == CMD.APPROVED && !!needSignature) {
    return !!handleModalForm.value.base64SignatureData;
  }
  return true;
});

// 处理流程弹窗表单评论label
const handleModalCommentLabel = (cmd) => {
  switch (cmd) {
    case CMD.APPROVED:
    case CMD.REJECTED:
    case CMD.ASSIGN:
    case CMD.ADD_BEFORE_SIGN:
    case CMD.ADD_AFTER_SIGN:
    case CMD.ADD_SIGN:
    case CMD.DEL_SIGN:
      return "审批意见";
    case CMD.CANCELED:
      return "撤回理由";
    case CMD.BACK:
      return "回退原因";
    case CMD.COMMENT:
      return "评论";
    case CMD.TRANSACT:
      return "办理意见";
  }
};

const onHandleModalOK = () => {
  // 取出上传的文件id
  let handleModalFormValue = ObjectUtil.copy(handleModalForm.value);
  let { flowCmd: cmd, fileIds } = handleModalFormValue;
  if (fileIds && fileIds.length > 0)
    handleModalFormValue.fileIds = fileIds.map((v) => v.id);

  let req = null;
  loading.value = true; // 开启遮罩
  switch (cmd) {
    case CMD.CANCELED:
      req = FlowInstApi.cancel(handleModalFormValue);
      break;
    case CMD.COMMENT:
      req = FlowInstApi.comment(handleModalFormValue);
      break;
    case CMD.BACK:
      req = FlowInstApi.jump(handleModalFormValue);
      break;
    case CMD.ADD_BEFORE_SIGN:
      req = FlowInstApi.addBeforeSign(handleModalFormValue);
      break;
    case CMD.ADD_AFTER_SIGN:
      req = FlowInstApi.addAfterSign(handleModalFormValue);
      break;
    case CMD.ADD_SIGN:
      req = FlowInstApi.addSign(handleModalFormValue);
      break;
    case CMD.DEL_SIGN:
      req = FlowInstApi.delSign(handleModalFormValue);
      break;
    case CMD.APPROVED:
      req = FlowInstApi.approve(handleModalFormValue);
      break;
    case CMD.REJECTED:
      req = FlowInstApi.reject(handleModalFormValue);
      break;
    case CMD.ASSIGN:
      req = FlowInstApi.assign(handleModalFormValue);
      break;
    case CMD.TRANSACT:
      req = FlowInstApi.transact(handleModalFormValue);
      break;
  }
  req
    .then((resp) => {
      if (resp.code == 1) {
        onHandleModalCancel();
        if (cmd == CMD.CANCELED) {
          props.flowInst.status = STATUS.CANCELLED;
          emits("update:flowInst", props.flowInst);
        }
        if (
          [
            CMD.ASSIGN,
            CMD.BACK,
            CMD.ADD_BEFORE_SIGN,
            CMD.ADD_AFTER_SIGN,
            CMD.APPROVED,
            CMD.REJECTED,
            CMD.TRANSACT,
          ].includes(cmd)
        ) {
          emits("onRemove");
        } else {
          loadFlowDetail();
        }
      }
      loading.value = false;
    })
    .catch((_) => (loading.value = false));
};

const initModalForm = (cmd) => {
  return {
    flowInstId: props.flowInst.id,
    taskId: props.flowInst.taskId,
    flowCmd: cmd,
    fileIds: [],
  };
};
const onApproved = () => {
  handleModalTitle.value = "同意审批";
  handleModalForm.value = initModalForm(CMD.APPROVED);
  showHandleModal.value = true;
};
const onRejected = () => {
  handleModalTitle.value = "拒绝审批";
  handleModalForm.value = initModalForm(CMD.REJECTED);
  showHandleModal.value = true;
};
const onTransacted = () => {
  handleModalTitle.value = "审批办理";
  handleModalForm.value = initModalForm(CMD.TRANSACT);
  showHandleModal.value = true;
};
const onCanceled = () => {
  handleModalTitle.value = "撤销审批";
  handleModalForm.value = initModalForm(CMD.CANCELED);
  showHandleModal.value = true;
};
const onAssigned = () => {
  handleModalTitle.value = "转交审批";
  handleModalForm.value = initModalForm(CMD.ASSIGN);
  showHandleModal.value = true;
};
const onComment = () => {
  handleModalTitle.value = "评论审批";
  handleModalForm.value = initModalForm(CMD.COMMENT);
  showHandleModal.value = true;
};
const onJumped = () => {
  FlowInstApi.listJumpableNodes({
    flowInstId: props.flowInst.id,
    actNodeId: props.flowInst.actNodeId,
  }).then((resp) => {
    if (resp.code == 1) jumpableNodes.value = resp.data || [];
  });
  handleModalTitle.value = "回退审批";
  handleModalForm.value = initModalForm(CMD.BACK);
  showHandleModal.value = true;
};
const onAddSigned = () => {
  handleModalTitle.value = "审批加签";
  handleModalForm.value = initModalForm(CMD.ADD_SIGN);
  showHandleModal.value = true;
};
const onDelSigned = () => {
  FlowInstApi.listRemoveableNodeAssignees({
    flowInstId: props.flowInst.id,
    actNodeId: props.flowInst.actNodeId,
  }).then((resp) => {
    if (resp.code == 1) deleteableUserIds.value = resp.data || [];
  });
  handleModalTitle.value = "审批减签";
  handleModalForm.value = initModalForm(CMD.DEL_SIGN);
  showHandleModal.value = true;
};

// 是否显示编辑记录按钮
const formEditRecordBtnVisible = ref(false);
const hasFormEditRecord = () => {
  FlowInstApi.hasFormEditRecord({ flowInstId: props.flowInst.id }).then((resp) => {
    if (resp.code == 1) formEditRecordBtnVisible.value = resp.data;
  });
};

// 再次申请相关
let launchVisible = ref(false);
let relaunchFlow = ref(); // 再次申请流程
let relaunchFlowForm = ref(); // 再次申请表单
// 关闭再次申请侧边栏
const onLaunchClose = () => {
  launchVisible.value = false;
};
// 再次申请
const onRelaunch = () => {
  FlowManApi.checkRelaunchable({ flowDefId: props.flowInst.flowDefId }).then((resp) => {
    let { data: flowDef } = resp;
    if (resp.code == 1 && flowDef && flowDef.id) {
      relaunchFlow.value = flowDef;
      relaunchFlowForm.value = ObjectUtil.copy(formValue.value);
      launchVisible.value = true;
    } else {
      Message.error("流程已经变更，不能再次申请！");
    }
  });
};

// 表单编辑相关
const formEditVisible = ref(false);
const formEditRecordVisible = ref(false);
const formEditable = computed(() => {
  let tmp = false;
  formWidgets.value.forEach((formWidget) => {
    if (formWidget.type == WIDGET.DETAIL) {
      formWidget.details.forEach((detail) => {
        if (detail.editable) tmp = true;
      });
    } else if (formWidget.editable) tmp = true;
  });
  return tmp;
});
const onFormEdit = () => {
  formEditVisible.value = true;
};
const onFormUpdated = (nv) => {
  let { formValue: value, formattedFormValue: formattedValue } = nv;
  formValue.value = JSON.parse(value);
  formattedFormValue.value = JSON.parse(formattedValue);
  hasFormEditRecord();
};
const onFormEditRecordClick = () => {
  formEditRecordVisible.value = true;
};

watch(
  () => props.flowInst,
  (nv) => {
    if (nv && nv.id && nv.flowDefId) {
      loadFlowDetail();
      loadFormWidgets();
      hasFormEditRecord();
    }
  },
  { immediate: true }
);

onMounted(() => {
  OrganApi.loadOrgan(); // 加载组织
});
</script>

<style lang="less" scoped>

        // gap: 8px;

  }
}

  transform: rotate(180deg);
}

  .arco-dropdown {
    padding: 4px;
  }
}

.flow-exe-box {
  .modify-sign-group {
    display: grid;
    grid-template-columns: 1fr 1fr 1fr;
    width: 100%;

    .modify-sign-tip {
      color: var(--color-text-4);
    }
  }

  .action-attachment {
    .arco-upload-list-item {
      margin-top: 0;

      &:first-of-type {
        margin-top: 12px;
      }

      .arco-upload-list-item-content {
        padding: 4px 10px 4px 12px;
      }

      .arco-upload-list-item-operation {
        .arco-icon {
          font-size: 16px;
        }
      }
    }

    .arco-upload-hide + .arco-upload-list .arco-upload-list-item:first-of-type {
      margin-top: 0px;
    }
  }
}
</style>
给出完整业务包含流程引擎的实现代码，不需要控制层代码，AppService即可作为接口访问层，同时需要注意前端显示设备二维码的功能，
需要在对应设备数据列表，用户点击详情详情，详情页面包含查看设备二维码功能以及简略设备用户信息，可供用户查看二维码信息
或点击打印按钮打印设备二维码（该二维码后续作为用户扫描可直接查看设备信息并可进行维修申报或进行保养的功能页面访问页），前端无需设定默认二维码值,
对应的操作功能不要使用到window.open这种方式进行操作
以下代码为封装好的上传附件组件

// src/api/biz/attachmentApi.js
import { baseRequest } from '@/utils/request'

const request = (url, ...arg) => baseRequest(`/api/services/app/Attachment/` + url, ...arg)

/**
 * 附件管理API
 */
export default {
    // 检查文件上传状态
    checkUpload(data) {
        return request('CheckUpload', data, 'post')
    },

    // 上传文件分片
    chunkUpload(data) {
        return request('ChunkUpload', data, 'post', {
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'multipart/form-data' }
        })
    },

    // 添加链接附件
    addLinkAttachment(data) {
        return request('AddLinkAttachment', data, 'post')
    },

    // 批量添加链接附件
    batchAddLinkAttachments(data) {
        return request('BatchAddLinkAttachments', data, 'post')
    },

    // 绑定附件到业务
    bindToBusiness(data) {
        return request('SetBusinessAttachments', data, 'post')
    },

    // 获取业务附件列表
    getBusinessAttachments(params) {
        return request('GetBusinessAttachments', params, 'get')
    },

    // 获取附件分页列表
    getPageList(params) {
        return request('GetPageList', params, 'get')
    },

    // 删除附件
    deleteAttachment(data,businessId) {
        return request(`Delete?businessId=${businessId}`, data, 'delete')
    },

    // 下载附件
    download(id) {
        const baseURL = baseRequest.defaults?.baseURL || ''
        return `${baseURL}/api/services/app/Attachment/Download?id=${id}`
    }
}

<!-- src/components/Attachment/index.vue -->

    <!-- 文件列表区域 -->
    <div class="file-list-container">

        <a-radio-group
          v-model:value="filterType"
          size="small"
          @change="handleFilterChange"
        >
          <a-radio-button :value="null">全部 ({{ totalCount }})</a-radio-button>
          <a-radio-button :value="0">本地文件 ({{ fileCount }})</a-radio-button>
          <a-radio-button :value="1">链接地址 ({{ linkCount }})</a-radio-button>
        </a-radio-group>
      </div>

      <!-- 上传中的文件列表 -->
      <template v-if="mode === 'edit' && uploadingFiles.length > 0">
        <div class="file-section-title">
          <span>上传中 ({{ uploadingFiles.length }})</span>
        </div>
        <div class="file-list">
          <div v-for="item in uploadingFiles" :key="item.uid" class="file-row uploading">
            <div class="file-info">
              <PaperClipOutlined class="file-icon" />
              <div class="file-detail">
                <div class="file-name">{{ item.fileName }}</div>

            <div class="file-progress">
              <a-progress
                :percent="item.percent"
                :show-info="false"
                size="small"

              />
              <span class="progress-text">{{ getProgressText(item) }}</span>
            </div>

            <div class="file-actions">
              <a-button
                v-if="item.status === 'error'"
                type="link"
                size="small"
                @click="retryUpload(item)"
              >
                <RedoOutlined />重试
              </a-button>
              <a-popconfirm

        </div>

        <!-- 表格形式的文件列表 -->

          >
            <!-- 文件名列 - 带图标和预览功能 -->
            <div class="file-col file-col-name">
              <div class="file-name-wrapper" @click="handleFileClick(file)">
                <component
                  :is="getFileIcon(file)"
                  class="file-type-icon"
                  :class="{ 'link-icon': file.attachmentType === 1 }"
                />
                <span class="file-name-text" :title="file.fileName">
                  {{ file.fileName }}
                </span>
                <span v-if="file.attachmentType === 1" class="link-badge">链接</span>
              </div>
            </div>

            <!-- 文件大小列 -->
            <div class="file-col file-col-size">
              <span class="file-size-text">
                {{ file.attachmentType === 1 ? "--" : formatFileSize(file.fileSize) }}
              </span>
            </div>

            <!-- 操作列 -->
            <div class="file-col file-col-actions">
              <div class="action-buttons">
                <!-- 下载按钮 -->
                <a-button
                  type="text"
                  size="small"
                  class="action-btn"
                  @click="downloadFile(file)"
                  :title="file.attachmentType === 1 ? '打开链接' : '下载'"
                  :loading="downloadingFileId === (file.attachmentId || file.id)"
                >
                  <template #icon>
                    <component
                      :is="
                        file.attachmentType === 1 ? 'LinkOutlined' : 'DownloadOutlined'
                      "
                    />
                  </template>
                  <span class="action-text">{{
                    file.attachmentType === 1 ? "打开" : "下载"
                  }}</span>
                </a-button>

                <!-- 删除按钮 - 只在编辑模式显示 -->
                <a-button
                  v-if="mode === 'edit'"
                  type="text"
                  danger
                  size="small"
                  class="action-btn"
                  @click="confirmDelete(file)"
                  title="删除"
                >
                  <template #icon><DeleteOutlined /></template>
                  <span class="action-text">删除</span>
                </a-button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </template>

      <!-- 空状态 -->
      <a-empty
        v-if="filteredFiles.length === 0 && uploadingFiles.length === 0"
        description="暂无附件"
      >
        <template #image>
          <FileOutlined :style="{ fontSize: '48px', color: '#bfbfbf' }" />
        </template>
      </a-empty>
    </div>

    <!-- 批量添加链接模态框 -->
    <a-modal
      v-model:visible="showBatchLinkModal"
      title="批量添加链接"
      width="600px"
      @ok="batchAddLinks"
      @cancel="resetBatchLinkForm"
      :confirmLoading="batchAddingLink"
    >
      <a-form layout="vertical" :model="batchLinkForm">
        <a-form-item
          label="链接列表（每行一个链接地址）"
          required
          :rules="[{ required: true, message: '请输入链接地址' }]"
        >
          <a-textarea
            v-model:value="batchLinkForm.links"
            placeholder="https://example.com/file1.pdf&#10;https://example.com/file2.docx&#10;https://example.com/image.jpg"
            :rows="6"
            allow-clear
          />
        </a-form-item>

        <a-form-item label="批量备注（可选）">
          <a-input
            v-model:value="batchLinkForm.remark"
            placeholder="所有链接共用的备注"
            allow-clear
          />

        <div class="batch-preview" v-if="batchLinkForm.links">
          <div class="preview-title">将添加 {{ linkList.length }} 个链接：</div>
          <div class="preview-list">
            <div v-for="(link, index) in linkList" :key="index" class="preview-item">
              <LinkOutlined /> {{ truncateUrl(link, 50) }}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </a-form>
    </a-modal>

    <!-- 文件预览模态框 - 只用于本地文件预览 -->
    <a-modal
      v-model:visible="previewVisible"
      :title="currentPreviewFile?.fileName"
      :footer="null"
      :width="previewWidth"
      :body-style="{ padding: 0, height: '80vh' }"
      centered
      @cancel="closePreview"
    >
      <!-- PDF预览 -->
      <div v-if="isPdf(currentPreviewFile)" class="pdf-preview">
        <vue-pdf-embed
          :source="getPdfSource()"
          @rendered="handlePdfRendered"
        />
        <div v-if="pdfPages > 1" class="pdf-pagination">
          <a-button-group>
            <a-button @click="prevPage" :disabled="currentPage <= 1">
              <LeftOutlined />
            </a-button>
            <a-button>{{ currentPage }} / {{ pdfPages }}</a-button>
            <a-button @click="nextPage" :disabled="currentPage >= pdfPages">
              <RightOutlined />
            </a-button>
          </a-button-group>
        </div>
      </div>

      <!-- Excel预览 -->
      <div v-else-if="isExcel(currentPreviewFile)" class="excel-preview">
        <div class="excel-toolbar">
          <a-select v-model:value="currentSheet" style="width: 200px">
            <a-select-option v-for="sheet in excelSheets" :key="sheet" :value="sheet">
              {{ sheet }}
            </a-select-option>
          </a-select>
          <a-button @click="downloadFile(currentPreviewFile)">下载原文件</a-button>
        </div>
        <div class="excel-content" ref="excelContainer"></div>
      </div>

      <!-- 图片预览 -->
      <div v-else-if="isImage(currentPreviewFile)" class="image-preview">
        <template v-if="!previewImageError">
          <img
            :src="previewImageUrl"
            :alt="currentPreviewFile?.fileName"
            class="preview-image"
            @load="handlePreviewImageLoad"
            @error="handlePreviewImageError"
          />
        </template>
        <template v-else>
          <div class="image-error-display">
            <FileImageOutlined :style="{ fontSize: '64px', color: '#ff4d4f' }" />
            <p>图片加载失败</p>
            <a-button type="primary" @click="downloadFile(currentPreviewFile)"
              >下载文件</a-button
            >
          </div>
        </template>
        <div v-if="previewImageLoading" class="image-loading">
          <a-spin tip="加载中..." />
        </div>
      </div>

      <!-- 文本文件预览 -->
      <div v-else-if="isTextFile(currentPreviewFile)" class="text-preview">
        <pre>{{ textContent }}</pre>
      </div>

      <!-- 其他文件预览 -->
      <div v-else class="unsupported-preview">
        <FileOutlined :style="{ fontSize: '64px', color: '#bfbfbf' }" />
        <p>该文件类型暂不支持在线预览</p>
        <a-button type="primary" @click="downloadFile(currentPreviewFile)"
          >下载文件</a-button
        >
      </div>

      <!-- 预览加载中 -->
      <div v-if="previewLoading" class="preview-loading">
        <a-spin tip="正在加载预览..." />
      </div>
    </a-modal>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup>
import { ref, computed, watch, nextTick, onUnmounted, reactive } from "vue";
import {
  InboxOutlined,
  PaperClipOutlined,
  DownloadOutlined,
  DeleteOutlined,
  EyeOutlined,
  CloseOutlined,
  RedoOutlined,
  LeftOutlined,
  RightOutlined,
  FileOutlined,
  FilePdfOutlined,
  FileWordOutlined,
  FileExcelOutlined,
  FilePptOutlined,
  FileZipOutlined,
  FileImageOutlined,
  FileTextOutlined,
  UploadOutlined,
  LinkOutlined,
  PlusOutlined,
  FileAddOutlined,
} from "@ant-design/icons-vue";
import { message, Modal } from "ant-design-vue";
import SparkMD5 from "spark-md5";
import attachmentApi from "@/api/biz/bizAttachmentApi";
import VuePdfEmbed from "vue-pdf-embed";
import * as XLSX from "xlsx";
import tool from "@/utils/tool";

const props = defineProps({
  // 模式：edit-编辑模式（可上传/删除），view-查看模式（只读）
  mode: {
    type: String,
    default: "view",
    validator: (value) => ["edit", "view"].includes(value),
  },
  // 业务ID
  businessId: {
    type: String,
    default: null,
  },
  // 业务类型
  businessType: {
    type: String,
    default: null,
  },
  // 附件列表（v-model）
  modelValue: {
    type: Array,
    default: () => [],
  },
  // 是否支持多文件上传
  multiple: {
    type: Boolean,
    default: true,
  },
  // 最大文件大小（MB）
  maxSize: {
    type: Number,
    default: 500,
  },
  // 支持的文件格式
  accept: {
    type: String,
    default: "*",
  },
  // 图片预览重试次数
  imageRetryCount: {
    type: Number,
    default: 3,
  },
  // 默认显示类型：null-全部，0-本地文件，1-链接地址
  defaultFilterType: {
    type: Number,
    default: null,
  },
  // 链接在新窗口打开（true）还是在当前窗口打开（false）
  linkOpenInNewWindow: {
    type: Boolean,
    default: true,
  },
});

const emit = defineEmits(["update:modelValue", "change", "success", "remove"]);

// 上传模式
const uploadMode = ref("file");

// 链接表单
const linkFormRef = ref(null);
const linkForm = reactive({
  linkUrl: "",
  fileName: "",
  remark: "",
});

const addingLink = ref(false);

// 批量链接
const showBatchLinkModal = ref(false);
const batchAddingLink = ref(false);
const batchLinkForm = reactive({
  links: "",
  remark: "",
});

// 类型筛选
const filterType = ref(props.defaultFilterType);

// 下载状态
const downloadingFileId = ref(null);

// 计算支持的文件格式文本
const supportFormats = computed(() => {
  if (props.accept === "*") return "所有格式";
  return props.accept.split(",").join("、");
});

// 上传文件列表（临时）
const uploadFileList = ref([]);
const uploadingFiles = ref([]);
const uploading = ref(false);

// 预览相关状态 - 仅用于本地文件
const previewVisible = ref(false);
const previewLoading = ref(false);
const currentPreviewFile = ref(null);
const previewFileUrl = ref("");
const previewWidth = ref("80%");
const previewImageLoading = ref(false);
const previewImageError = ref(false);
const previewImageUrl = ref("");
const previewImageRetryCount = ref(0);

// PDF预览相关
const currentPage = ref(1);
const pdfPages = ref(0);

// Excel预览相关
const excelSheets = ref([]);
const currentSheet = ref("");
const excelContainer = ref(null);

// 文本预览内容
const textContent = ref("");

// 显示的文件列表（已上传的）
const displayFiles = computed(() => {
  return props.modelValue.map((file) => ({
    ...file,
    id: file.attachmentId || file.id,
    uid: file.uid || `file-${file.id || Date.now()}`,
    imageLoading: file.imageLoading || false,
    imageError: file.imageError || false,
    imageRetryCount: file.imageRetryCount || 0,
    attachmentType:
      file.attachmentType ||
      (file.linkUrl ||
      (file.filePath &&
        (file.filePath.startsWith("http://") || file.filePath.startsWith("https://")))
        ? 1
        : 0),
  }));
});

// 统计
const totalCount = computed(() => displayFiles.value.length);
const fileCount = computed(
  () => displayFiles.value.filter((f) => f.attachmentType === 0).length
);
const linkCount = computed(
  () => displayFiles.value.filter((f) => f.attachmentType === 1).length
);

// 过滤后的文件列表
const filteredFiles = computed(() => {
  if (filterType.value === null) {
    return displayFiles.value;
  }
  return displayFiles.value.filter((f) => f.attachmentType === filterType.value);
});

// 链接列表（批量添加）
const linkList = computed(() => {
  if (!batchLinkForm.links) return [];
  return batchLinkForm.links
    .split("\n")
    .map((line) => line.trim())
    .filter(
      (line) => line && (line.startsWith("http://") || line.startsWith("https://"))
    );
});

// 图片扩展名列表
const IMAGE_EXTENSIONS = [".jpg", ".jpeg", ".png", ".gif", ".bmp", ".webp", ".svg"];
const PDF_EXTENSIONS = [".pdf"];
const EXCEL_EXTENSIONS = [".xls", ".xlsx", ".csv"];
const WORD_EXTENSIONS = [".doc", ".docx"];
const PPT_EXTENSIONS = [".ppt", ".pptx"];
const TEXT_EXTENSIONS = [
  ".txt",
  ".md",
  ".json",
  ".xml",
  ".yml",
  ".yaml",
  ".js",
  ".css",
  ".html",
];

// 获取token
const getToken = () => {
  return tool.data.get("TOKEN");
};

// 判断文件类型
const isImage = (file) => {
  if (!file?.fileName) return false;
  const ext = file.fileName.substring(file.fileName.lastIndexOf(".")).toLowerCase();
  return IMAGE_EXTENSIONS.includes(ext);
};

const isPdf = (file) => {
  if (!file?.fileName) return false;
  const ext = file.fileName.substring(file.fileName.lastIndexOf(".")).toLowerCase();
  return PDF_EXTENSIONS.includes(ext);
};

const isExcel = (file) => {
  if (!file?.fileName) return false;
  const ext = file.fileName.substring(file.fileName.lastIndexOf(".")).toLowerCase();
  return EXCEL_EXTENSIONS.includes(ext);
};

const isWord = (file) => {
  if (!file?.fileName) return false;
  const ext = file.fileName.substring(file.fileName.lastIndexOf(".")).toLowerCase();
  return WORD_EXTENSIONS.includes(ext);
};

const isTextFile = (file) => {
  if (!file?.fileName) return false;
  const ext = file.fileName.substring(file.fileName.lastIndexOf(".")).toLowerCase();
  return TEXT_EXTENSIONS.includes(ext);
};

// 获取文件图标
const getFileIcon = (file) => {
  if (!file?.fileName) return FileOutlined;

  // 链接文件特殊处理
  if (file.attachmentType === 1) return LinkOutlined;

  const ext = file.fileName.substring(file.fileName.lastIndexOf(".")).toLowerCase();

  const iconMap = {
    ".pdf": FilePdfOutlined,
    ".doc": FileWordOutlined,
    ".docx": FileWordOutlined,
    ".xls": FileExcelOutlined,
    ".xlsx": FileExcelOutlined,
    ".ppt": FilePptOutlined,
    ".pptx": FilePptOutlined,
    ".zip": FileZipOutlined,
    ".rar": FileZipOutlined,
    ".7z": FileZipOutlined,
    ".jpg": FileImageOutlined,
    ".jpeg": FileImageOutlined,
    ".png": FileImageOutlined,
    ".txt": FileTextOutlined,
    ".md": FileTextOutlined,
    ".json": FileTextOutlined,
  };

  return iconMap[ext] || FileOutlined;
};

// 获取带token的预览URL（用于图片等直接通过src加载的资源）
const getAuthorizedPreviewUrl = (file, timestamp = Date.now()) => {
  const id = file.attachmentId || file.id;
  if (!id) return "";

  const baseURL = import.meta.env.VITE_API_BASEURL || "";
  const url = `${baseURL}/api/services/app/Attachment/Download?id=${id}`;
  const token = getToken();

  if (token) {
    const separator = url.includes("?") ? "&" : "?";
    return `${url}${separator}authorization=Bearer ${encodeURIComponent(
      token
    )}&_t=${timestamp}`;
  }
  return url;
};

// 获取带token的下载URL（用于fetch请求）
const getAuthorizedDownloadUrl = (file) => {
  const id = file.attachmentId || file.id;
  if (!id) return "";

  const baseURL = import.meta.env.VITE_API_BASEURL || "";
  return `${baseURL}/api/services/app/Attachment/Download?id=${id}`;
};

// 获取PDF的source配置（带请求头）
const getPdfSource = () => {
  if (!currentPreviewFile.value) return null;

  const fileId = currentPreviewFile.value.attachmentId || currentPreviewFile.value.id;
  if (!fileId) return null;

  const baseURL = import.meta.env.VITE_API_BASEURL || "";
  const url = `${baseURL}/api/services/app/Attachment/Download?id=${fileId}`;
  const token = getToken();

  return {
    url: url,
    httpHeaders: token
      ? {
          Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
        }
      : undefined,
    withCredentials: false,
  };
};

// 处理文件点击（预览或打开）
const handleFileClick = (file) => {
  if (file.attachmentType === 1 || file.linkUrl) {
    openLink(file);
  } else {
    previewFile(file);
  }
};

// 截断URL
const truncateUrl = (url, maxLength = 40) => {
  if (!url) return "";
  if (url.length <= maxLength) return url;
  return url.substring(0, maxLength) + "...";
};

// 格式化文件大小
const formatFileSize = (bytes) => {
  if (!bytes || bytes === 0) return "0 B";
  const k = 1024;
  const sizes = ["B", "KB", "MB", "GB"];
  const i = Math.floor(Math.log(bytes) / Math.log(k));
  return parseFloat((bytes / Math.pow(k, i)).toFixed(2)) + " " + sizes[i];
};

// 获取进度文本
const getProgressText = (item) => {
  if (item.status === "calculating") return "计算MD5...";
  if (item.status === "merging") return "合并中...";
  if (item.status === "error") return "上传失败";
  if (item.status === "success") return "上传成功";
  return Math.round(item.percent) + "%";
};

// 更新上传文件项的进度
const updateFileProgress = (fileItem, percent, status) => {
  fileItem.percent = percent;
  if (status) {
    fileItem.status = status;
  }
  uploadingFiles.value = [...uploadingFiles.value];
};

// 添加链接附件
const addLinkAttachment = async () => {
  try {
    // 表单验证
    if (!linkForm.linkUrl) {
      message.warning("请输入链接地址");
      return;
    }

    // URL验证
    try {
      new URL(linkForm.linkUrl);
    } catch {
      message.error("请输入有效的URL地址");
      return;
    }

    addingLink.value = true;

    const params = {
      linkUrl: linkForm.linkUrl,
      fileName: linkForm.fileName || undefined,
      remark: linkForm.remark || undefined,
    };

    const result = await attachmentApi.addLinkAttachment(params);

    if (result) {
      // 获取附件详情
      const newAttachment = {
        id: result,
        attachmentId: result,
        fileName: linkForm.fileName || extractFileNameFromUrl(linkForm.linkUrl),
        fileSize: 0,
        fileSizeFormat: "0 B",
        attachmentType: 1,
        linkUrl: linkForm.linkUrl,
        filePath: linkForm.linkUrl,
        creationTime: new Date().toISOString(),
      };

      // 添加到列表
      emit("update:modelValue", [...props.modelValue, newAttachment]);
      emit("change", newAttachment);
      emit("success", newAttachment);

      message.success("链接添加成功");

      // 重置表单
      resetLinkForm();
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("添加链接失败:", error);
    message.error(error.message || "添加链接失败");
  } finally {
    addingLink.value = false;
  }
};

// 批量添加链接
const batchAddLinks = async () => {
  if (!batchLinkForm.links) {
    message.warning("请输入链接地址");
    return;
  }

  const links = linkList.value;
  if (links.length === 0) {
    message.warning("没有有效的链接地址");
    return;
  }

  batchAddingLink.value = true;

  try {
    const params = links.map((url) => ({
      linkUrl: url,
      remark: batchLinkForm.remark || undefined,
    }));

    const result = await attachmentApi.batchAddLinkAttachments(params);

    if (result) {
      // 获取所有新添加的附件详情
      const newAttachments = result.map((id, index) => ({
        id,
        attachmentId: id,
        fileName: extractFileNameFromUrl(links[index]),
        fileSize: 0,
        fileSizeFormat: "0 B",
        attachmentType: 1,
        linkUrl: links[index],
        filePath: links[index],
        creationTime: new Date().toISOString(),
      }));

      // 添加到列表
      emit("update:modelValue", [...props.modelValue, ...newAttachments]);

      if (result.message) {
        message.warning(result.message);
      } else {
        message.success(`成功添加 ${newAttachments.length} 个链接`);
      }
    }

    // 关闭模态框并重置
    showBatchLinkModal.value = false;
    resetBatchLinkForm();
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("批量添加链接失败:", error);
    message.error(error.message || "批量添加链接失败");
  } finally {
    batchAddingLink.value = false;
  }
};

// 从URL提取文件名
const extractFileNameFromUrl = (url) => {
  try {
    const parsed = new URL(url);
    const pathname = parsed.pathname;
    const fileName = pathname.substring(pathname.lastIndexOf("/") + 1);

    if (fileName && fileName.includes(".")) {
      return decodeURIComponent(fileName);
    }

    // 如果没有文件名，使用域名+时间戳
    return `${parsed.hostname}_${new Date().getTime()}.link`;
  } catch {
    return `link_${new Date().getTime()}.link`;
  }
};

// 重置链接表单
const resetLinkForm = () => {
  linkForm.linkUrl = "";
  linkForm.fileName = "";
  linkForm.remark = "";
};

// 重置批量链接表单
const resetBatchLinkForm = () => {
  batchLinkForm.links = "";
  batchLinkForm.remark = "";
};

// 处理类型筛选变化
const handleFilterChange = () => {
  // 触发更新
};

// 打开链接（前端直接打开）
const openLink = (file) => {
  const url = file.linkUrl || file.filePath;
  if (!url) {
    message.warning("链接地址不存在");
    return;
  }

  if (props.linkOpenInNewWindow) {
    window.open(url, "_blank");
  } else {
    window.location.href = url;
  }
};

// 处理图片加载错误（列表中的缩略图）
const handleImageError = (event, file) => {
  console.error("图片加载失败:", file.fileName, event);

  const fileIndex = props.modelValue.findIndex(
    (f) => (f.attachmentId || f.id) === (file.attachmentId || file.id)
  );
  if (fileIndex !== -1) {
    const updatedFiles = [...props.modelValue];
    const targetFile = updatedFiles[fileIndex];

    const retryCount = (targetFile.imageRetryCount || 0) + 1;

    if (retryCount <= props.imageRetryCount) {
      setTimeout(() => {
        const img = event.target;
        if (img) {
          const newUrl = getAuthorizedPreviewUrl(file, Date.now());
          img.src = newUrl;
        }
      }, 1000 * retryCount);

      targetFile.imageRetryCount = retryCount;
      targetFile.imageLoading = true;
    } else {
      targetFile.imageError = true;
      targetFile.imageLoading = false;
    }

    emit("update:modelValue", updatedFiles);
  }
};

// 处理图片加载成功
const handleImageLoad = (file) => {
  const fileIndex = props.modelValue.findIndex(
    (f) => (f.attachmentId || f.id) === (file.attachmentId || file.id)
  );
  if (fileIndex !== -1) {
    const updatedFiles = [...props.modelValue];
    updatedFiles[fileIndex].imageLoading = false;
    updatedFiles[fileIndex].imageError = false;
    updatedFiles[fileIndex].imageRetryCount = 0;
    emit("update:modelValue", updatedFiles);
  }
};

// 上传前处理
const beforeUpload = async (file) => {
  // 检查文件大小
  const maxBytes = props.maxSize * 1024 * 1024;
  if (file.size > maxBytes) {
    message.error(`文件 ${file.name} 大小不能超过 ${props.maxSize}MB`);
    return false;
  }

  // 检查是否已存在相同文件
  const existingFile = displayFiles.value.find(
    (f) => f.fileName === file.name && f.fileSize === file.size
  );
  if (existingFile) {
    message.warning(`文件 ${file.name} 已存在`);
    return false;
  }

  // 创建上传文件项
  const fileItem = {
    uid: file.uid,
    fileName: file.name,
    fileSize: file.size,
    status: "calculating",
    percent: 0,
    file: file,
    chunks: [],
    identifier: null,
    attachmentId: null,
    abortController: new AbortController(),
    uploadedChunks: [],
  };

  uploadingFiles.value.push(fileItem);

  // 开始处理文件
  processFile(fileItem);

  return false;
};

// 处理文件
const processFile = async (fileItem) => {
  try {
    // 计算MD5
    updateFileProgress(fileItem, 0, "calculating");

    const md5 = await calculateFileMD5(fileItem.file, (progress) => {
      updateFileProgress(fileItem, Math.round(progress * 100));
    });

    fileItem.identifier = md5;
    updateFileProgress(fileItem, 100);

    // 检查文件是否已存在
    const checkResult = await checkFileExists(fileItem);

    if (checkResult.uploaded) {
      // 秒传
      fileItem.status = "success";
      fileItem.percent = 100;
      fileItem.attachmentId = checkResult.attachmentId;
      message.success(`文件 ${fileItem.fileName} 上传成功(秒传)`);

      // 添加到已上传列表
      addToUploadedList(fileItem);
      return;
    }

    // 记录已上传的分片
    fileItem.uploadedChunks = checkResult.uploadedChunks || [];

    // 分片上传
    await uploadFileInChunks(fileItem, fileItem.uploadedChunks);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("处理文件失败:", error);
    updateFileProgress(fileItem, 0, "error");
    fileItem.error = error.message;
  }
};

// 计算文件MD5
const calculateFileMD5 = (file, onProgress) => {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const chunkSize = 2 * 1024 * 1024; // 2MB
    const chunks = Math.ceil(file.size / chunkSize);
    let currentChunk = 0;
    const spark = new SparkMD5.ArrayBuffer();
    const fileReader = new FileReader();

    fileReader.onload = (e) => {
      spark.append(e.target.result);
      currentChunk++;

      onProgress?.(currentChunk / chunks);

      if (currentChunk < chunks) {
        loadNext();
      } else {
        resolve(spark.end());
      }
    };

    fileReader.onerror = () => {
      reject(new Error("文件读取失败"));
    };

    const loadNext = () => {
      const start = currentChunk * chunkSize;
      const end = Math.min(start + chunkSize, file.size);
      fileReader.readAsArrayBuffer(file.slice(start, end));
    };

    loadNext();
  });
};

// 检查文件是否已上传
const checkFileExists = async (fileItem) => {
  try {
    const chunkSize = 5 * 1024 * 1024;
    const totalChunks = Math.ceil(fileItem.file.size / chunkSize);

    const params = {
      fileIdentifier: fileItem.identifier,
      fileName: fileItem.fileName,
      totalSize: fileItem.fileSize,
      totalChunks: totalChunks,
    };

    const resData = await attachmentApi.checkUpload(params);
    return resData;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("检查文件失败:", error);
    return { uploaded: false, uploadedChunks: [] };
  }
};

// 分片上传
const uploadFileInChunks = async (fileItem, uploadedChunks) => {
  updateFileProgress(fileItem, fileItem.percent, "uploading");

  const chunkSize = 5 * 1024 * 1024; // 5MB
  const totalChunks = Math.ceil(fileItem.file.size / chunkSize);

  // 计算已上传的分片
  let uploadedCount = uploadedChunks.length;
  updateFileProgress(fileItem, Math.round((uploadedCount / totalChunks) * 100));

  // 按顺序上传每个分片
  for (let i = 1; i <= totalChunks; i++) {
    // 跳过已上传的分片
    if (uploadedChunks.includes(i)) continue;

    // 检查是否已取消
    if (fileItem.abortController.signal.aborted) {
      updateFileProgress(fileItem, 0, "error");
      fileItem.error = "上传已取消";
      return;
    }

    try {
      const start = (i - 1) * chunkSize;
      const end = Math.min(start + chunkSize, fileItem.file.size);
      const chunkFile = fileItem.file.slice(start, end);

      const formData = new FormData();
      formData.append("FileIdentifier", fileItem.identifier);
      formData.append("ChunkNumber", i);
      formData.append("ChunkSize", chunkSize);
      formData.append("CurrentChunkSize", end - start);
      formData.append("TotalChunks", totalChunks);
      formData.append("FileName", fileItem.fileName);
      formData.append("FileType", fileItem.file.type);
      formData.append("TotalSize", fileItem.fileSize);
      formData.append("File", chunkFile);

      await attachmentApi.chunkUpload(formData, {
        signal: fileItem.abortController.signal,
      });

      // 记录已上传的分片
      fileItem.uploadedChunks.push(i);
      uploadedCount++;
      updateFileProgress(fileItem, Math.round((uploadedCount / totalChunks) * 100));

      // 强制刷新视图
      await nextTick();
    } catch (error) {
      if (error.name === "AbortError" || error.code === "ERR_CANCELED") {
        updateFileProgress(fileItem, 0, "error");
        fileItem.error = "上传已取消";
        return;
      }

      console.error(`分片 ${i} 上传失败:`, error);
      updateFileProgress(fileItem, fileItem.percent, "error");
      fileItem.error = `分片 ${i} 上传失败`;

      // 询问是否重试
      const shouldRetry = await showRetryDialog(fileItem.fileName, i);
      if (shouldRetry) {
        uploadedCount--; // 重试当前分片
        i--; // 重新上传当前分片
        updateFileProgress(fileItem, fileItem.percent, "uploading");
        continue;
      }
      return;
    }
  }

  // 所有分片上传完成，检查合并状态
  updateFileProgress(fileItem, 99, "merging");

  // 轮询检查文件是否合并完成
  let checkCount = 0;
  const maxChecks = 30;

  while (checkCount < maxChecks) {
    await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));

    try {
      const checkResult = await checkFileExists(fileItem);
      if (checkResult.uploaded) {
        updateFileProgress(fileItem, 100, "success");
        fileItem.attachmentId = checkResult.attachmentId;

        message.success(`文件 ${fileItem.fileName} 上传成功`);
        addToUploadedList(fileItem);
        return;
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("检查文件状态失败:", error);
    }

    checkCount++;
  }

  // 超时
  updateFileProgress(fileItem, 0, "error");
  fileItem.error = "文件合并超时";
};

// 显示重试对话框
const showRetryDialog = (fileName, chunkNumber) => {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    Modal.confirm({
      title: "上传失败",
      content: `文件 ${fileName} 分片 ${chunkNumber} 上传失败，是否重试？`,
      okText: "重试",
      cancelText: "取消",
      onOk: () => resolve(true),
      onCancel: () => resolve(false),
    });
  });
};

// 添加到已上传列表
const addToUploadedList = (fileItem) => {
  // 从上传列表中移除
  const index = uploadingFiles.value.findIndex((f) => f.uid === fileItem.uid);
  if (index > -1) {
    uploadingFiles.value.splice(index, 1);
  }

  // 添加到已上传列表
  const newFile = {
    uid: fileItem.uid,
    attachmentId: fileItem.attachmentId,
    fileName: fileItem.fileName,
    fileSize: fileItem.fileSize,
    id: fileItem.attachmentId,
    attachmentType: 0,
    imageLoading: false,
    imageError: false,
    imageRetryCount: 0,
  };

  emit("update:modelValue", [...props.modelValue, newFile]);
  emit("change", newFile);
  emit("success", newFile);
};

// 重试上传
const retryUpload = (fileItem) => {
  fileItem.status = "calculating";
  fileItem.percent = 0;
  fileItem.error = null;
  fileItem.attachmentId = null;
  fileItem.abortController = new AbortController();
  fileItem.uploadedChunks = [];
  processFile(fileItem);
};

// 取消上传并清理已上传的分片
const cancelUpload = async (fileItem) => {
  // 中止上传
  if (fileItem.abortController) {
    fileItem.abortController.abort();
  }

  // 清理已上传的分片
  if (fileItem.identifier && fileItem.uploadedChunks.length > 0) {
    try {
      const hideLoading = message.loading(
        `正在清理 ${fileItem.fileName} 的上传记录...`,
        0
      );

      await attachmentApi.cleanupChunks({
        fileIdentifier: fileItem.identifier,
        chunks: fileItem.uploadedChunks,
      });

      hideLoading();
      message.success(`已清理 ${fileItem.fileName} 的上传记录`);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("清理上传记录失败:", error);
      message.warning(`清理上传记录失败，但上传已取消`);
    }
  }

  // 从上传列表中移除
  const index = uploadingFiles.value.findIndex((f) => f.uid === fileItem.uid);
  if (index > -1) {
    uploadingFiles.value.splice(index, 1);
  }
};

// 确认删除
const confirmDelete = (file) => {
  Modal.confirm({
    title: "确认删除",
    content: `确定要删除文件 "${file.fileName}" 吗？`,
    okText: "确定",
    cancelText: "取消",
    onOk: () => handleDelete(file),
  });
};

// 删除文件
const handleDelete = async (file) => {
  const fileId = file.attachmentId || file.id;
  console.log(props.businessId);
  const businessId = props.businessId;
  try {
    // 调用后端删除接口
    if (fileId) {
      await attachmentApi.deleteAttachment([{ id: fileId }], businessId);
    }

    // 从列表中移除
    const newList = props.modelValue.filter(
      (f) => (f.attachmentId || f.id) !== fileId && f.uid !== file.uid
    );

    emit("update:modelValue", newList);
    emit("remove", file);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("删除文件失败:", error);
  }
};

// 下载文件
const downloadFile = async (file) => {
  const fileId = file.attachmentId || file.id;
  if (!fileId) {
    message.error("文件ID不存在");
    return;
  }

  // 如果是链接附件，直接打开链接
  if (file.attachmentType === 1 || file.linkUrl) {
    openLink(file);
    return;
  }

  if (downloadingFileId.value === fileId) {
    return;
  }

  downloadingFileId.value = fileId;

  try {
    const url = getAuthorizedDownloadUrl(file);
    const token = getToken();

    const response = await fetch(url, {
      headers: token ? { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` } : {},
    });

    if (!response.ok) {
      if (response.status === 401) {
        throw new Error("未授权，请重新登录");
      }
      throw new Error(`下载失败 (${response.status})`);
    }

    const contentType = response.headers.get("Content-Type");
    if (contentType && contentType.includes("application/json")) {
      const errorData = await response.json();
      throw new Error(errorData.error?.message || errorData.message || "下载失败");
    }

    const blob = await response.blob();

    const contentDisposition = response.headers.get("Content-Disposition");
    let fileName = file.fileName;
    if (contentDisposition) {
      const matches = /filename[^;=\n]*=((['"]).*?\2|[^;\n]*)/.exec(contentDisposition);
      if (matches && matches[1]) {
        fileName = matches[1].replace(/['"]/g, "");
        try {
          fileName = decodeURIComponent(fileName);
        } catch (e) {}
      }
    }

    const link = document.createElement("a");
    link.href = window.URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    link.download = fileName;
    document.body.appendChild(link);
    link.click();
    window.URL.revokeObjectURL(link.href);
    document.body.removeChild(link);

    message.success("下载完成");
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("下载失败:", error);
    message.error(error.message || "下载失败");
  } finally {
    downloadingFileId.value = null;
  }
};

// 预览文件（仅本地文件）
const previewFile = async (file) => {
  // 如果是链接附件，直接打开
  if (file.attachmentType === 1 || file.linkUrl) {
    openLink(file);
    return;
  }

  currentPreviewFile.value = file;
  previewVisible.value = true;
  previewLoading.value = true;

  if (isPdf(file)) {
    previewWidth.value = "70%";
  } else if (isExcel(file)) {
    previewWidth.value = "80%";
    await previewExcel(file);
  } else if (isImage(file)) {
    previewWidth.value = "auto";
    previewImageLoading.value = true;
    previewImageError.value = false;
    previewImageRetryCount.value = 0;
    previewImageUrl.value = getAuthorizedPreviewUrl(file, Date.now());
  } else if (isTextFile(file)) {
    previewWidth.value = "60%";
    await previewText(file);
  } else {
    previewWidth.value = "50%";
  }

  previewLoading.value = false;
};

// 预览Excel
const previewExcel = async (file) => {
  try {
    const url = getAuthorizedDownloadUrl(file);
    const token = getToken();

    const response = await fetch(url, {
      headers: token ? { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` } : {},
    });

    if (!response.ok) {
      if (response.status === 401) {
        throw new Error("未授权，请重新登录");
      }
      throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
    }

    const arrayBuffer = await response.arrayBuffer();
    const workbook = XLSX.read(arrayBuffer, { type: "array" });

    excelSheets.value = workbook.SheetNames;
    currentSheet.value = workbook.SheetNames[0];

    renderExcelSheet(workbook, currentSheet.value);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("预览Excel失败:", error);
    message.error("Excel预览失败: " + error.message);
    previewVisible.value = false;
  }
};

// 渲染Excel工作表
const renderExcelSheet = (workbook, sheetName) => {
  if (!excelContainer.value) return;

  const sheet = workbook.Sheets[sheetName];
  const html = XLSX.utils.sheet_to_html(sheet, {
    id: "excel-table",
    editable: false,
  });

  excelContainer.value.innerHTML = html;
};

// 预览文本文件
const previewText = async (file) => {
  try {
    const url = getAuthorizedDownloadUrl(file);
    const token = getToken();

    const response = await fetch(url, {
      headers: token ? { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` } : {},
    });

    if (!response.ok) {
      if (response.status === 401) {
        throw new Error("未授权，请重新登录");
      }
      throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
    }

    textContent.value = await response.text();
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("预览文本文件失败:", error);
    message.error("文本预览失败: " + error.message);
    previewVisible.value = false;
  }
};

// 预览图片加载成功
const handlePreviewImageLoad = () => {
  previewImageLoading.value = false;
  previewLoading.value = false;
};

// 预览图片加载失败
const handlePreviewImageError = () => {
  previewImageLoading.value = false;
  previewImageError.value = true;
  previewLoading.value = false;
};

// 重试预览图片
const retryPreviewImage = () => {
  if (previewImageRetryCount.value < props.imageRetryCount) {
    previewImageRetryCount.value++;
    previewImageLoading.value = true;
    previewImageError.value = false;
    previewImageUrl.value = getAuthorizedPreviewUrl(currentPreviewFile.value, Date.now());
  } else {
    message.warning("已达到最大重试次数");
  }
};

// 关闭预览
const closePreview = () => {
  previewVisible.value = false;
  currentPreviewFile.value = null;
  previewFileUrl.value = "";
  previewImageLoading.value = false;
  previewImageError.value = false;
  previewImageRetryCount.value = 0;
  previewImageUrl.value = "";
  textContent.value = "";
  excelSheets.value = [];
  currentSheet.value = "";
  currentPage.value = 1;
  pdfPages.value = 0;
};

// PDF翻页
const prevPage = () => {
  if (currentPage.value > 1) {
    currentPage.value--;
  }
};

const nextPage = () => {
  if (currentPage.value < pdfPages.value) {
    currentPage.value++;
  }
};

const handlePdfRendered = (pdf) => {
  pdfPages.value = pdf.numPages;
  previewLoading.value = false;
};



// 自定义上传请求
const customRequest = ({ file, onSuccess, onError, onProgress }) => {
  // 已通过 beforeUpload 处理
};

const handleDrop = (event) => {};

// 暴露方法
defineExpose({
  getFiles: () => displayFiles.value,
  getFilteredFiles: () => filteredFiles.value,
  clear: () => {
    uploadingFiles.value.forEach((item) => {
      if (item.abortController) {
        item.abortController.abort();
      }
      if (item.identifier && item.uploadedChunks.length > 0) {
        attachmentApi
          .cleanupChunks({
            fileIdentifier: item.identifier,
            chunks: item.uploadedChunks,
          })
          .catch(console.error);
      }
    });
    uploadingFiles.value = [];
  },
  setFilterType: (type) => {
    filterType.value = type;
  },
});

// 监听businessId变化，加载附件
watch(
  () => props.businessId,
  async (newVal) => {
    if (newVal && props.businessType) {
      try {
        const params = {
          businessId: newVal,
          businessType: props.businessType,
        };

        // 如果设置了默认筛选类型，也传入
        if (filterType.value !== null) {
          params.attachmentType = filterType.value;
        }

        const res = await attachmentApi.getBusinessAttachments(params);
        // 为每个文件添加图片状态字段
        const filesWithState = (res || []).map((file) => ({
          ...file,
          imageLoading: false,
          imageError: false,
          imageRetryCount: 0,
          attachmentType: file.attachmentType || (file.linkUrl ? 1 : 0),
        }));
        emit("update:modelValue", filesWithState);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("加载附件列表失败:", error);
      }
    }
  },
  { immediate: true }
);

// 监听默认筛选类型变化
watch(
  () => props.defaultFilterType,
  (newVal) => {
    filterType.value = newVal;
  },
  { immediate: true }
);

// 组件卸载时清理所有上传中的文件
onUnmounted(() => {
  uploadingFiles.value.forEach((item) => {
    if (item.abortController) {
      item.abortController.abort();
    }
    if (item.identifier && item.uploadedChunks.length > 0) {
      attachmentApi
        .cleanupChunks({
          fileIdentifier: item.identifier,
          chunks: item.uploadedChunks,
        })
        .catch(console.error);
    }
  });
});
</script>
